44013052	Taalibaaɓe ɓee kebbinaa seyo e Ruuhu Ceniiɗo.
44014001	Ley Ikoniya duu Pool e Barnabas naati e ley waajordu Yahuudiyankooɓe. Eɓe mbaajoo faa Yahuudiyankooɓe e yimɓe leɲi goɗɗi heewɓe ngoonɗini.
44014002	Kaa Yahuudiyankooɓe saliiɓe goonɗinde ɓee loofi leɲi goɗɗi ɗii, mbonni ɓerɗe muuɗum'en yalla ana mbaɲa sakiraaɓe ɓee.
44014003	Ɗum e taweede haɗaali ɓe ɓooyde ton, eɓe pawi jikke maɓɓe e Joomiraaɗo, eɓe mbaajoroo cuusal. Joomiraaɗo seettii konngol hinnee muuɗum, nde hokkunoo ɓe baawɗe waɗude taagumansaaji e kaayɗe dogooje e juuɗe maɓɓe.
44014004	Yimɓe ngeenndi ndii ɓee peccii: yoga heedani Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee, yoga heedani nelaaɓe ɓee.
44014005	Yimɓe leɲi goɗɗi e Yahuudiyankooɓe e ardiiɓe muuɗum'en anniyii torrude ɓe e wardude ɓe kaaƴe.
44014006	Nde ɓe maatunoo ɗum ndee, ɓe ndogani Listara e Derbe e geelle seraaji muuɗum'en ley leydi Likoniya,
44014007	eɓe mbaajoo ton Kabaaru Lobbo oo.
44014008	Gorko bonnguujo, dimdaaɗo e bonnguwaaku, mo meeɗaali daraade e koyɗe muuɗum, ana wonnoo Listara.
44014009	Omo hettinoo waaju Pool. Pool ƴeewi mo, yii goonɗinal makko sellinta mo,
44014010	haaldi semmbe, wii: --Imma, dara e koyɗe maa! Gorko oo gurbitii, darii, ana yaha.
44014011	Nde yimɓe ɓee njii ko Pool waɗi koo ndee, ngulliri gullaali likoniyankoore, mbii: --Laamɗo'en nanndinkinike e yimɓe, njippiima e meeɗen!
44014012	Ɓe inndiri Barnabas "Jewus", ɓe inndiri Pool "Hermes", sabi Pool wonnoo kaaloowo.
44014013	Galle ɗo Jewus rewetee ana wonnoo to naatirde ngeenndi too. Jottinoowo sadaka oo waddi ga'i pariraaɗi piindi e dame ɗee. Omo yiɗi waɗude sadaka, kanko e yimɓe ɓee.
44014014	Kaa nde Barnabas e Pool nannoo ɗum ndee, ceeki kaddule muuɗum'en, keɲanii jamaa oo ana ngulla,
44014015	ana mbiya: --Worɓe, koɗum ngaɗaton ɗoo? Minen duu min yimɓe hono mooɗon. Miɗen mbaajoo Kabaaru Lobbo oo faa tuubon, iwon e ɗii golleeji laaliiɗi, ngarton e Laamɗo guurɗo, taguɗo kammu e leydi e geeci e ko woni e muuɗum'en fuu.
44014016	E jamaanuuji jawtuɗi ɗii o yoppii leɲi ɗii fuu njokka laawi muuɗum'en.
44014017	Ɗum e taweede, omo golla ko moƴƴi faa ɗum seettanoo mo, omo hokka on toɓo kammu, omo ɓenndinana on ɲamri e wakkati muuɗum, omo waaltinira hakkillaaji mon nguure e seyo.
44014018	Ko ɓe mbaajii koo fuu, semmbe ɓe kaɗiri jamaa oo hokkude ɓe sadaka.
44014019	Caggal ɗum, Yahuudiyankooɓe iwi Antiyokiya e Ikoniya. Ɓe keɓi hakkillaaji yimɓe ɓee, ɓeen mbedii Pool kaaƴe, ndaasi ɗum faa naɓi ɗum caggal ngeenndi ndii, sabi miilii mo maayɗo.
44014020	Kaa nde taalibaaɓe ɓee ngari pilii mo ndee, o immii, o naatti e ley ngeenndi ndii. Janngo muuɗum, o yaadi e Barnabas ngeenndi mbiyeteendi Derbe.
44014021	Ɓe mbaajii ton Kabaaru Lobbo oo, ɓe keɓi taalibaaɓe faa keewi. Caggal muuɗum, ɓe mbirfitii Listara e Ikoniya, kaɲum e Antiyokiya.
44014022	Eɓe cuusina yonkiiji taalibaaɓe, eɓe mbaajoo ɗum'en yo ɲiiɓu e goonɗinal, eɓe mbiya: --Kinaa tampen tampereeji keewɗi so naaten e Laamu Laamɗo.
44014023	E ley deente goonɗinɓe ɗee fuu, ɓe cuɓanii ɗum'en hooreeɓe. Caggal ɗum, ɓe koori, ɓe nduwii, ɓe kalfini ɗum'en Joomiraaɗo mo ɓe ngoonɗini oo.
44014024	Nde ɓe ceekunoo Pisidiya ndee, ɓe ngari Pamfiliya.
44014025	Ɓe mbaajii konngol ngol ley ngeenndi Perge. Caggal muuɗum, ɓe njippoyii Attaliya.
44014026	Ton ɓe naati laana geeci, ɓe mbirfii Antiyokiya ɗo ɓe kalfinanoo moƴƴere Laamɗo faa ɓe ngolla golle mo ɓe tilii jooni oo.
44014027	Nde ɓe njottinoo ndee, ɓe mooɓti deental goonɗinɓe ngal, ɓe kaalani ngal ko Laamɗo waɗidi e maɓɓe fuu, no o udditirani yimɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe damal goonɗinal.
44014028	Ɓe ngondi ɗon e taalibaaɓe ɓee faa ɓooyi.
44015001	Yimɓe yogaaɓe iwi Yahuudiya ngari Antiyokiya, ana njanngina sakiraaɓe ɓee, ana mbiya: --So on taadiraaka no Muusaa wiiri nii, on kisataa.
44015002	Pool e Barnabas pooɗondiri e maɓɓe, nduddi e maɓɓe faa naawi. Ɗum waɗi so ɓe tabintini nelde Pool e Barnabas e yimɓe woɓɓe faa Urusaliima, faade e nelaaɓe ɓee e hooreeɓe ɓee, saabe haala kaa.
44015003	Ɗum saabii so deental goonɗinɓe ngal neli ɓe. Ɓe ceeki Finikiya e Samariya, eɓe kaalana ɗum'en haala tuubugol yimɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe. Ɗum laatanii sakiraaɓe ɓee fuu seyo manngo.
44015004	Nde ɓe njottinoo Urusaliima ndee, deental goonɗinɓe ngal e nelaaɓe ɓee e hooreeɓe ɓee njaɓɓii ɓe. Ɓe kaalani ɗum'en ko Laamɗo waɗani ɓe fuu.
44015005	Kaa yoga e goonɗinɓe jeyaaɓe e fedde Farisa'en immii, mbii: --Waajibi ɓe taadee, ɓe njamiree jokkude Sariya Muusaa oo.
44015006	Nelaaɓe ɓee e mawɓe ɓee kawriti faa ƴeewa haala kaa.
44015007	Caggal haali-haalti keewɗo, Piyeer immii, wii ɓe: --Sakiraaɓe, oɗon anndi Laamɗo suɓike kam e ley mooɗon gila ko ɓooyi, faa mi waajoo Kabaaru Lobbo oo hakkunde yimɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe, yalla eɓe nana ɓe ngoonɗina.
44015008	Laamɗo annduɗo ɓerɗe oo hollii jaɓanii ɓe, nde hokki ɓe Ruuhu Ceniiɗo oo hono no meeɗen nii.
44015009	Walaa fuu ko o seenndiri en e maɓɓe, nde wonnoo o laɓɓinirii ɓerɗe maɓɓe goonɗinal.
44015010	Jooni, ko saabii so oɗon itta koro Laamɗo? Oɗon pawa e taalibaaɓe ɓee donngal, ngal enen e maamiraaɓe meeɗen en mbaawaa roondaade.
44015011	E moƴƴere Joomiraaɗo men Iisaa ngoonɗinir-ɗen so kisu-ɗen, hono non kamɓe duu.
44015012	Deental ngal fuu deƴƴinii teen, ana hettinoo Barnabas e Pool ana njantoo no Laamɗo waɗiri taagumansaaji e kaayɗe hakkunde leɲi goɗɗi.
44015013	Caggal ɓe ndeƴƴinike, Yaakuuba jaɓɓitii, wii: --Sakiraaɓe, kettinanee kam!
44015014	Simon humpitii en no Laamɗo suɓorii gila e puɗɗooɗe yimɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe, faa waɗa ɗum'en yimɓe muuɗum.
44015015	Ɗum hawri e haalaaji annabaaɓe ɗii, hono no winndiraa nii:
44015016	"Joomiraaɗo wii: Caggal ɗum, mi wartan, mi mahitoo suudu Daawuuda saamundu nduu, mi reentinan taƴe tuufeeje ɗee, mi darna ndu kasen,
44015017	yalla yimɓe heddiiɓe ɓee ana tewta Joomiraaɗo. Ɗum woni, leɲi ɗi innde am noddaa e muuɗum'en ɗii. Joomiraaɗo tabintinɗo ɗeen kulle
44015018	anndaaɗe gila huunde fuu tagaaka, wii non."
44015019	Ɗum saabii miin kaa ko njii-mi, pati tiiɗinanen yimɓe leɲi goɗɗi tuubuɓe so ngarti e Laamɗo ɓee.
44015020	Kaa ko haani hen, nelen e maɓɓe ɓe nantoo e ko tooruuji coɓini e jeenu e ɲaamde jiibe e ɲaamde ƴiiƴam.
44015021	Gila e jamaanuuji ɓooyɗi, Sariya Muusaa ana jannginee ley geelle ɗee fuu, eɓe njannga mo ɲalaande fowteteende fuu ley cuuɗi baajorɗi.
44015022	Ɗum waɗi so nelaaɓe ɓee kaɲum e hooreeɓe ɓee e deental goonɗinɓe ngal fuu ndawridi faa cuɓoo worɓe e ley muuɗum'en faa nela ɗum'en Antiyokiya, ɓe tawta Pool e Barnabas. Ɓe cuɓii hooreeɓe ɗiɗon ley sakiraaɓe ɓee, Yahuuda noddirteeɗo Barasaba, kaɲum e Silas.
44015023	Ɓe ndokki ɗum'en oo ɗoo ɓataaki: Minen sakiraaɓe mooɗon, nelaaɓe kaɲum e hooreeɓe, miɗen njowta on, onon sakiraaɓe amen leɲi goɗɗi wonɓe Antiyokiya e Siriya e Silisi.
44015024	Min nanii yimɓe iwii ga amen girƴinirii on haalaaji, njiiɓii hakkillaaji mon. Minen nee, min njamiraali ɓe.
44015025	Min ndawridii, min kawrii, min cuɓike worɓe faa min nela ɗum'en e mooɗon, ɓe tawta yiɓɓe amen Barnabas e Pool,
44015026	yeebiiɓe yonkiiji muuɗum'en saabe Joommen Iisaa Almasiihu.
44015027	Ɗum waɗi so min neli Yahuuda e Silas, pammina on ko min mbinndi e mon koo hunduko e hunduko.
44015028	Minen e Ruuhu Ceniiɗo, min kawrii pati min njappa on ko teddi so wanaa ko tilsi koo:
44015029	nanto-ɗon e kirsanaaɗi tooruuji e ƴiiƴam e jiibuɗi e jeenu. So on ndeenii ko'e mon e majji, on ngaɗii ko moƴƴi. Yo Laamɗo faabo en!
44015030	Ɓe ndokkaa laawol, ɓe njehi Antiyokiya. Nde ɓe njottinoo ndee, ɓe mooɓti deental goonɗinɓe ngal, ɓe ndokki ngal ɓataaki oo.
44015031	Nde ɓeen janngunoo mo ndee, ceyii sabi haalaaji ɗii ndokkii ɗum'en semmbe.
44015032	Yahuuda e Silas, Laamɗo loowi e mum'en konngol mum faa ɓe mbaajii sakiraaɓe waajuuji keewɗi, cuusini ɗum'en.
44015033	Caggal ɓe paɓɓii ton, ɓe ceerti e sakiraaɓe ɓee e dow jam, ɓe mbirfitii to nelnooɓe ɓee too. [
44015034	]
44015035	Pool e Barnabas njooɗii ley Antiyokiya ana njanngina ana mbaajoo konngol Joomiraaɗo. Woɓɓe heewɓe ana mballa ɓe.
44015036	Caggal balɗe seeɗa, Pool wii Barnabas: --Mbirfo-ɗen e geelle ɗe mbaajino-ɗen konngol Joomiraaɗo ngol ɗee fuu, njippano-ɗen sakiraaɓe meeɗen ɓee, ƴeewen no ɓe ngorri.
44015037	Barnabas ana yiɗunoo ɓe njaada e Yuhanna noddirteeɗo Marka.
44015038	Kaa ɗum welaali Pool sabi oon seeriino e maɓɓe Pamfiliya yaadaali e maɓɓe faa gollida e maɓɓe.
44015039	Barnabas e Pool mettondiri faa ceerti. Homo e maɓɓe fuu suɓii neɗɗo goɗɗo. Barnabas yaadi e Marka, naati laana geeci feewi Kiprus.
44015040	Pool suɓii Silas, yaadi e muuɗum caggal sakiraaɓe ɓee kalfinii ɗum e hinnee Joomiraaɗo.
44015041	O seeki Siriya e Silisi, omo yaha omo hokka deente goonɗinɓe ɗee semmbe.
44016001	Pool wari Derbe, caggal ɗum, o yottii Listara. Goonɗinɗo biyeteeɗo Timote ana wonnoo ɗon. Inniiko yo Yahuudiyanke goonɗinɗo, kaa baam makko yo Yunaninke.
44016002	Sakiraaɓe wonɓe Listara e Ikoniya ɓee ana njetta mo.
44016003	Pool yiɗi naɓorde mo, taadi mo, nde wonnoo Yahuudiyankooɓe hoɗuɓe e ɗeen leyɗe ɓee fuu ana anndi baam makko yo Yunaninke.
44016004	Ley geelle ɗe ɓe ceeki ɗee, eɓe njottina goonɗinɓe ɓee sariya mo nelaaɓe e mawɓe wonɓe Urusaliima ɓee ɓami oo, eɓe njamira ɓeen yo njokku mo.
44016005	Hono non, deente goonɗinɓe ɗee ana ɓeydoroo semmbe banngal goonɗinal, ana ɓeydoo heewde ɲannde fuu.
44016006	Ruuhu Ceniiɗo haɗi ɓe waajaade konngol ngol ley Asiya, saabe majjum ɓe ceeki leydi Firigiya e leydi Galaatiya.
44016007	Nde ɓe ngarnoo keerol Misiya ndee, ɓe tewti yaade Bitiniya, kaa Ruuhu Iisaa yarranaaki ɓe ɓe naata.
44016008	E ley ɗum, ɓe ƴaɓɓii Misiya, ɓe ndegii e ngeenndi mbiyeteendi Torowas.
44016009	E ley jemmaaku muuɗum won ko ƴellitii e Pool. O yii gorko Makedoniyanke ana darii, ana ndaarda mo ana wiya: --Lummbu, ngaraa Makedoniya paabo-ɗaa min!
44016010	Nde Pool yiinoo won ko ƴellitii e mum ndee, oon wakkati fuu min ndaari yaade Makedoniya, min taƴori Laamɗo noddi min faa min mbaajoo ɓe Kabaaru Lobbo oo.
44016011	Hono non, min naati laana geeci iwde Torowas, min paati ruunde Samotaras. Janngo muuɗum, min pahi Neyapolis.
44016012	Min iwi ɗon, min pahi Filipa, ngeenndi ɓurndi fuu teentilaade e leydi Makedoniya ndi Romankooɓe kumanii. Min ngaɗi ɗon balɗe.
44016013	Ɲalaande fowteteende, min njaltiri ngeenndi ndii hedde daande maayo, ton Yahuudiyankooɓe mboownoo waɗude duwaawu. Min tawi ɗon rewɓe ana mooɓtii, min njooɗii, min mbaajii ɓe.
44016014	Debbo dewoowo Laamɗo, biyeteeɗo Lidiya, coottoowo kaddule boɗeeje, jeyaaɗo ngalluure wiyeteende Tiyatira, ana hettinoo. Joomiraaɗo udditi ɓernde makko yalla omo goonɗina ko Pool waajotoo koo.
44016015	Kanko e koreeji makko fuu ɓe lootaa lootogal batisima. Caggal ɗum, o ɲaagii min, o wii: --So oɗon njogorii kam mi goonɗinɗo Joomiraaɗo, njippee suudu am. O tilsini min njippanoo mo.
44016016	Ɲannde wootere miɗen njahannoo to nokkuure waɗirde duwaawu. Korɗo debbo bataaɗo annduɗo ko warata hawriti e amen. Halfaaɓe makko paggike kaalisi keewɗo e ndaggadaaku makko oo.
44016017	Mo jokki e amen, minen e Pool, omo wulla, omo wiya: --Ɓee yimɓe yo gollanooɓe Laamɗo Toowɗo oo! Eɓe mbaajoo on laawol kisindam.
44016018	Balɗe kuurɗe omo waɗa non faa Pool mettaa, yeeccitii, wii ladde ndee: --Saabe Iisaa Almasiihu, yaltu e makko! Ladde ndee yalti oon wakkati fuu.
44016019	Nde halfaaɓe ɓee anndunoo jikke muuɗum'en iwii e faggitoraade korɗo oo ndee, nanngi Pool e Silas, ndaasi ɗum'en faa sakoro to sarooɓe.
44016020	Non ɓe naɓi ɓeen to hooreeɓe ngeenndi ndii, mbii: --Ɓee worɓe ɗiɗon ɓe Yahuudiyankooɓe, eɓe nii ngadda baasi e ngeenndi meeɗen ndii.
44016021	Eɓe mbaajoo aadaaji ɗi ndagantaako en njaɓen naa ngollen, enen Romankooɓe.
44016022	Jamaa oo diirani ɓe. Hooreeɓe ɓee njamiri kaddule maɓɓe ceekee, ɓe piyee.
44016023	Ɓe piyaa faa naawi, ɓe uddaa ley kasu. Hooreeɓe ɓee njamiri kayboowo kasu oo hayba ɓe faa gasa.
44016024	Oon nee, gila heɓi ndee yamiroore, naanni ɓe e ley suudu kasu hakkundeeru, o geƴƴii koyɗe maɓɓe geƴƴelle leɗɗe.
44016025	Nde hejjere jemma warnoo ndee, Pool e Silas ana ndewa Laamɗo, eɓe njaaroo ɗum. Kasunkooɓe woɓɓe ɓee ana kettinanoo ɓe.
44016026	Oon wakkati fuu, leydi dimmbii dimmbagol manngol faa pooɓe kasu ɗee njergi. Dame ɗee fuu udditii, geƴƴelle kasunkooɓe ɗee fuu kumtii.
44016027	Nde kayboowo oo finnoo so yii dame kasu ɗee ana udditii ndee, soorti kaafaawi muuɗum faa wartoo, miili kasunkooɓe ɓee ndogii.
44016028	Pool wulli faa toowi, wii mo: --Pati waɗu hoore maa fay huunde ko boni, min fuu miɗen ɗoo!
44016029	Nde o heɓunoo fooyre ndee, o dogani kasu to Pool e Silas ngoni too, o sujidi, hedde omo siɲɲa.
44016030	Caggal ɗum, o yaltini ɓe, o wii ɓe: --Baabiraaɓe, hono fuu kaan-mi waɗude yalla miɗo hisa?
44016031	Ɓe njaabii mo, ɓe mbii: --Goonɗin Iisaa Joomiraaɗo oo faa kisaa, aan e koreeji maa.
44016032	Ɓe mbaajii mo konngol Joomiraaɗo ngol, kanko e koreeji makko fuu.
44016033	Oon jemma fuu o naɓi ɓe, o lootoyi barme maɓɓe. Oon wakkati fuu o lootaa lootogal batisima, kanko e koreeji makko fuu.
44016034	O naanni Pool e Silas suudu makko, o hokki ɗum'en ɲaamdu. Kanko e koreeji makko fuu ɓe ceyii sabi ɓe keɓii goonɗinde Laamɗo.
44016035	Nde weetunoo ndee, hooreeɓe Romankooɓe ɓee neli laamunkooɓe mbiya kayboowo oo yoppa worɓe ɗiɗon ɓee.
44016036	Kayboowo oo haalanoyi ɗum Pool, wii: --Hooreeɓe ɓee nelii njoppite-ɗon. Njalton jooni, yo on njottoyo e jam.
44016037	Pool jaabii, wii: --Ɓe njamirii min piyee yeeso yimɓe tawee min caraaka, ɓe naanni min e kasu. Minen worɓe ɗiɗon ɓee, min fuu min Romankooɓe. Jooni ɓe yaltinirooɓe min cuucuukka naa? Patti, ɗum waawaa laataade. Kinaa kamɓe e ko'e maɓɓe, ɓe ngara ɓe njaltina min!
44016038	Laamunkooɓe ɓee kaaltani hooreeɓe Romankooɓe ɓee haala kaa. Ɓeen kuli nde nannoo Pool e Silas yo Romankooɓe ndee.
44016039	Ɓe njehi, ɓe curoyi ɓeen, ɓe njaltini ɗum'en kasu oo. Ɓe ndaardi ɗum'en njaltana ɓe ngeenndi ndii.
44016040	Nde Pool e Silas njaltunoo e kasu oo ndee, naati galle Lidiya. Ɓe njii sakiraaɓe ɓee, ɓe mbaaltini hakkillaaji mum'en. Caggal ɗum, ɓe mbitti.
44017001	Pool e Silas ceeki Amfipolis e Apolloni, njottii Tesaloniiki, toon duu waajordu Yahuudiyankooɓe won.
44017002	Pool waɗi no woowri nii, naati e ley waajordu nduu. Ɲalaaɗe powteteeɗe tati omo liddondira e maɓɓe omo dallinoroo Binndi ɗii.
44017003	O fammini ɓe, o holli ɓe ana tilsi Almasiihu oo torree, immintinee e maayde. O wii ɓe: --Iisaa mo mbaajotoo-mi on haala muuɗum oo, kaɲum woni Almasiihu.
44017004	Yoga e maɓɓe taƴori ɗum goonga, njokki e Pool e Silas, kaɲum e Yunaninkooɓe rewooɓe Laamɗo heewɓe e rewɓe saahiiɓe yonɓe.
44017005	Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓe nganaa goonɗinɓe ɓee konnii Pool e Silas, nanngi yimɓe laaliiɓe yiilotooɓe ley sakoro, ndeentini ɗum'en. Ɓe njirkiti ngalluure ndee fuu. Ɓe naati e galle Yason, eɓe tewta Pool e Silas faa ɓe naɓa ɗum'en to yimɓe ɓee too.
44017006	Nde ɓe ndonki yiitude ɓeen ndee, ɓe ndaasi Yason e yoga e sakiraaɓe ɓee faa to saranooɓe ngalluure ndee, eɓe ngulla eɓe mbiya: --Yimɓe imminooɓe baasi e aduna oo fuu ngarii ɗoo,
44017007	Yason jippinii ɗum'en! Ɓe fuu ko ɓe ngaɗata koo ana luuttondiri e sariya kaananke Roma mawɗo oo, eɓe mbiya ana woodi kaananke goɗɗo biyeteeɗo Iisaa.
44017008	Ɗiin haalaaji njirkiti jamaa oo e saranooɓe ngalluure ndee ɓee.
44017009	Yason e sakiraaɓe ɓee njoɓi kaalisi, caggal muuɗum ɓe njoppitaa.
44017010	Oon wakkati fuu e ley jemmaaku muuɗum, sakiraaɓe ɓee neli Pool e Silas Bereya. Nde ɓe njottii ndee, ɓe njehi to waajordu Yahuudiyankooɓe too.
44017011	Ɓeen ɓuri Yahuudiyankooɓe wonɓe Tesaloniiki ɓee laaɓude ɓernde. Ɓe njaɓɓorii konngol ngol soobee, eɓe mbiɗoo Binndi ɗii ɲannde fuu faa ɓe ƴeewa yalla ko Pool waajii koo yo goonga.
44017012	Heewɓe e maɓɓe ngoonɗini, kaɲum e rewɓe Yunaninkooɓe saahiiɓe e worɓe Yunaninkooɓe heewɓe.
44017013	Nde Yahuudiyankooɓe Tesaloniiki ɓee anndunoo Pool waajike konngol Laamɗo ngol ley Bereya ndee, ɓe ngari ton, ɓe njiiɓi jamaa oo.
44017014	Oon wakkati fuu, sakiraaɓe ɓee neli Pool faa maayo geeci, Silas e Timote keddii ɗon.
44017015	Liwndiiɓe Pool ɓee njaadi e muuɗum faa Ateena. Ɓe ngarti, ɓe ngaddani Silas e Timote nelal ngara to Pool law.
44017016	Nde Pool doomannoo ɓe Ateena fade maɓɓe warde ndee, yonki muuɗum ɲawi sanne ko yii no ngalluure ndee foti heewde tooruuji nii.
44017017	Ɗum waɗi so o haaldi e Yahuudiyankooɓe e rewooɓe Laamɗo woɓɓe ley waajordu nduu, omo haalda e ɓe o hawrannoo e mum ɲannde fuu ley sakoro ɓee duu.
44017018	Yoga e miijotooɓe wiyeteeɓe Epikuri'en e Sitoyko'en njaabondiri e makko. Yogaaɓe ana mbiya: --Koɗum oo ndorƴoowo haalata? Woɓɓe duu ana mbiya: --Omo nanndi e baajotooɗo haala tooruuji janani. Walaa ko ɓe mbiiri non so wanaa haala Iisaa kaɲum e immital maayɓe o waajinoo ɓe.
44017019	Nden ɓe ɓami Pool ɓe naɓi ɗum waamnde haayre wiyeteende Areyopagus, ɓe mbii ɗum: --Miɗen njiɗi anndude diina keso mo mbaajoto-ɗaa oo.
44017020	Sabi a toɓɓii e noppi amen haalaaji ɗi min mboowaa nande. Miɗen njiɗi anndude maanaa majji.
44017021	Tawi Ateenankooɓe e hoɓɓe jooɗiiɓe ton ɓee ngollataa huunde fuu so wanaa haalde huunde heyre nde ɓe nani.
44017022	Nden Pool darii hakkunde Areyopagus, wii: --Ateenankooɓe, mi yii e mon on diinankooɓe sanne,
44017023	sabi nde njiilinoo-mi e ngalluure mooɗon ndee, mi yii cuuɗi mooɗon dewirɗi, mi tawii ana winndaa e ittirde sadaka wootere: "laamɗo mo anndaaka". Ndennoo, ko ndewaton ko on anndaa koo, ɗum mbaajotoo-mi on e muuɗum.
44017024	Laamɗo taguɗo aduna e ko woni e muuɗum fuu oo, kaɲum woni Jom kammu e leydi, o jooɗataako ley cuuɗi mahiraaɗi juuɗe.
44017025	O hasindinaa e yimɓe ngollana mo fay huunde, sabi kanko hokkata tageefu oo fuu nguurndam e yonki e foofaango e huunde fuu.
44017026	E neɗɗo gooto Laamɗo yaltini leɲi ɗii fuu, joƴƴini ɗum'en e aduna oo. Gila ɗum waɗaali, o darnani ɗum'en jamaanuuji e keeri hakkunde koɗorɗe muuɗum'en,
44017027	yalla eɓe tewta Laamɗo, ɓe moomoo faa ɓe njiita ɗum. Ɗum e taweede o woɗɗaaki fay gooto e meeɗen.
44017028	"Nguurndam e dillinaade e goodal, saabe makko keɓir-ɗen." No yoga e yimooɓe mooɗon mbii: "Enen duu, en iwdi makko."
44017029	Nde wonnoo en iwdi makko, en kaanaa miijaade omo nanndi e tooru moƴƴiniraandu kaŋŋe naa kaalisi naa haayre sehaande, nde neɗɗo moƴƴinirta ɲeeɲal e hakkille.
44017030	Laamɗo rewtaaki yimɓe nde ngonnoo e majjere ndee. Jooni, o yamirii yimɓe fuu tuuba ɗo tawaa fuu,
44017031	sabi o sartike wakkati mo o sarirta aduna oo e fooccitaare, o sarira ɗum neɗɗo mo o suɓii oo. O hollii yimɓe fuu ɗum yo goonga nde o immintini oon neɗɗo e maayde.
44017032	Nde ɓe nannoo Pool ana waajoo haala immital maayɓe ndee, yoga ana uƴƴoo mo, yoga ana wiya: --Min kettinante oo waaju ɲannde wonnde.
44017033	Non Pool iwi hakkunde maɓɓe.
44017034	Yoga jokkii e makko, goonɗinii. Ana jeyaa e ɓeen biyeteeɗo Diyonisiyus, jeyaaɗo e deental Areyopagus, kaɲum e debbo biyeteeɗo Damaris, e woɓɓe kasen.
44018001	Caggal ɗum, Pool iwi Ateena, yehi Korintu.
44018002	O tawi ton Yahuudiyanke biyeteeɗo Akilas, pinɗo leydi mbiyeteendi Ponta. Ɓooyaali ko oon e jom suudu muuɗum biyeteeɗo Piriskilla iwi Italiya, sabi Kalawdiyus kaananke mawɗo oo yamiriino Yahuudiyankooɓe fuu njalta Roma. Pool yehi ƴeewoyde ɓe.
44018003	O woni ɗon, omo gollida e maɓɓe sabi o moƴƴinoowo hukkummaaji no maɓɓe nii.
44018004	Ɲalaande fowteteende fuu, Pool ana liddondira e Yahuudiyankooɓe e Yunaninkooɓe ley waajordu, yalla omo heɓa hakkillaaji maɓɓe.
44018005	Nde Silas e Timote iwnoo Makedoniya njottii Korintu ndee, Pool watti hakkille muuɗum fuu e waajaade, ana seettanoo Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee Iisaa woni Almasiihu oo.
44018006	Kaa nde wonnoo eɓe calanii mo, eɓe njennannoo mo, o fiɗɗi kaddule makko, o wii ɓe: --Yo diina mon fiito on! Mi walaa hen hannde, mi walaa hen janngo. Gila jooni mi yahan to ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe.
44018007	O iwi ɗon, o yehi to gorko dewoowo Laamɗo, biyeteeɗo Titus Yustus, mo galle muuɗum takkii e waajordu nduu.
44018008	Kirispus, hooreejo waajordu nduu oo, kaɲum e koreeji muuɗum fuu ngoonɗini Joomiraaɗo. Heewɓe e Korintunkooɓe hettintonooɓe ɓee ngoonɗini, lootaa lootogal batisima.
44018009	Jemma gooto Joomiraaɗo ƴellintini e Pool, wii: --Pati hul, pati deƴƴina, waaja.
44018010	Miɗo wondi e maa. Fay gooto waawaa torrude ma, sabi yimɓe am ana keewi ley ndee ngalluure.
44018011	Pool jooɗii hakkunde maɓɓe hitaande e feccere, ana janngina ɓe konngol Laamɗo ngol.
44018012	Nde Galliyon laaminoo leydi Akaya ndee, Yahuudiyankooɓe kaaldi, kawri, nanngi Pool, naɓi ɗum sarirde,
44018013	kappi ɗum, mbii: --Oo gorko yo ƴoɲɲoowo yimɓe yalla ana ndewra Laamɗo ko waldaa e sariya oo.
44018014	Pool anniyii faa haala, forri Galliyon wii Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee: --Yahuudiyankooɓe, so tawii tooɲannge naa golle bonɗo, mi jaɓanan on ko ngullani-ɗon mo koo,
44018015	kaa nde wonnoo ɗum jeddi dow haalaaji diina mooɗon e inɗe, kaɲum e sariya mooɗon onon tan, ɗum onon e ko'e mooɗon carata. Miin, mi sarataa ɗee kuɗɗe!
44018016	O yaltini ɓe sarirde ndee.
44018017	Nden, ɓe fuu ɓe nanngi Sosteni, hooreejo waajordu nduu oo, ɓe pii ɗum ɗo yeeso sarirde ɗoo. Kaa fuu Galliyon ɓilaaki hen fey.
44018018	Pool faɓɓi ɗon balɗe kuurɗe. Caggal ɗum, o waynondiri e sakiraaɓe ɓee, o naati laana, o feewi Siriya, kanko e Piriskilla e Akilas. Fade makko naatude, tawi o laɓii hoore makko nokku biyeteeɗo Kankiriya sabi o fodiino fodoore.
44018019	Ɓe njottii Efeesu, Pool yoppi ɗon Piriskilla e Akilas, kaɲum naati waajordu ana liddondira e Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee.
44018020	Ɓe ndaardi mo o faɓɓana ɓe, kaa o jaɓaali.
44018021	Nde o waynondirta e maɓɓe ndee, o wii: --Mi wartan e mooɗon so Laamɗo jaɓii. O naati laana, o iwi Efeesu,
44018022	o yottii Kaysariya, o ŋabbiti Urusaliima faa o jowta deental goonɗinɓe ngal. Caggal ɗum, o yehi Antiyokiya.
44018023	Caggal Pool waɗii ton wakkati, o witti. O seeki leydi Galaatiya e leydi Firigiya, omo yaha omo ɓeydana taalibaaɓe cuusal.
44018024	Yahuudiyanke biyeteeɗo Apollos, pinɗo Aleksandiri, wari Efeesu. O gorko fasiilante haala, baawɗo Binndi ɗii,
44018025	annduɗo laawol Joomiraaɗo. Omo waajoroo soobirantaaku e seyo, diina Iisaa kaa pay o jannginta. Kaa o anndaa so wanaa lootogal batisima Yaayaa ngal.
44018026	Omo waajoroo cuusal e ley waajordu nduu. Nde Piriskilla e Akilas kettinaninoo mo ndee, ɓe naɓi mo, ɓe pirritani mo laawol Laamɗo ngol faa ɓuri no arannde nii laaɓude.
44018027	Nde Apollos anniyinoo yaade leydi Akaya ndee, sakiraaɓe ɓee mballi mo, ɓe mbinndi e taalibaaɓe wonɓe ton ɓee ɓataaki njaɓɓoo mo faa gasa. Nde o yottii ton ndee, o walli goonɗinɓe ɓee e dow moƴƴere Laamɗo sanne.
44018028	Sabi o liɓii Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee ngattu naawɗo hakkunde yimɓe, omo dallinoroo Binndi ɗii, omo tabintina Iisaa woni Almasiihu.
44019001	Nde Apollos wonnoo Korintu ndee, Pool jokki laawol haayre, yehi Efeesu. O tawi ton taalibaaɓe,
44019002	o lamndii ɗum'en, o wii: --Yalla on keɓiino Ruuhu Ceniiɗo oo nde ngoonɗin-ɗon ndee naa? Ɓe njaabii mo: --Min nanaali Ruuhu Ceniiɗo ana woodi duu, sako min keɓa.
44019003	O lamndii ɓe, o wii: --Ndennoo, lootogal batisima hongal keɓu-ɗon? Ɓe njaabii, ɓe mbii: --Lootogal batisima Yaayaa ngal.
44019004	Pool wii: --Yaayaa batisima tuubugol batisannoo, ana wiya yimɓe ɓee yo ngoonɗin garoowo caggal muuɗum oo, ɗum woni Iisaa.
44019005	Nde ɓe nannoo ɗum ndee, ɓe mbatisiraa saabe Iisaa Joomiraaɗo oo.
44019006	Nde Pool fawnoo juuɗe muuɗum e maɓɓe ndee, Ruuhu Ceniiɗo jippii e maɓɓe, eɓe kaala e ɗemɗe janane, eɓe kaalta ko Laamɗo loowi e maɓɓe koo.
44019007	Eɓe mbaara e yimɓe sappo e ɗiɗon.
44019008	Pool naati e ley waajordu nduu, ana waajoroo ɓe cuusal hakke lebbi tati, omo haalda e maɓɓe, omo liddondira e maɓɓe, omo haɓanoo famminde ɓe haala Laamu Laamɗo.
44019009	Kaa tiiɗuɓe ko'e ngon e maɓɓe, calii goonɗinde, ana mbonnita laawol Joomiraaɗo ngol yeeso yimɓe fuu. Ɗum waɗi so Pool seerti e maɓɓe, naɓi taalibaaɓe ɓee feere, ana waajoo ɗum'en ɲannde fuu e ley janngirde neɗɗo biyeteeɗo Tirannus.
44019010	O worri non faa hiɓɓi duuɓi ɗiɗi, faa hoɗunooɓe e Asiya ɓee fuu, gila e Yahuudiyankooɓe faa e Yunaninkooɓe, nani konngol Joomiraaɗo ngol.
44019011	Laamɗo waɗiri juuɗe Pool kaayɗe mawɗe,
44019012	fay e sarbetiiji e kaddule memnooɗe terɗe makko ana naɓee pawee e ɲawɓe, ɲawuuji muuɗum'en cella, seyɗaani'en njalta e muuɗum'en.
44019013	Yoga e Yahuudiyankooɓe yiilotooɓe faa ndibba seyɗaani'en, ndaarii ribbirde ɗum'en innde Iisaa, mbii: --Alhorma Iisaa mo Pool waajotoo haala muuɗum oo, njaltee!
44019014	Gooto e hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka, Yahuudiyanke biyeteeɗo Sikewas, ɓiɓɓe muuɗum worɓe njeɗɗon ngaɗii non,
44019015	faa seyɗaani jaabii ɗum'en, wii: --Miɗo anndi Iisaa, miɗo anndi Pool, kaa onon, on hoɓe?
44019016	Neɗɗo laddaaɗo oo haɓi e maɓɓe, jaalii ɓe, torri ɓe faa ɓe ndogi, ɓe njaltiri galle oo terɗe teete e barme.
44019017	Kabaaru majjum saakii hakkunde Yahuudiyankooɓe e Yunaninkooɓe jooɗiiɓe Efeesu. Kulol nanngi ɓe fuu, innde Iisaa Joomiraaɗo oo teddinaa.
44019018	Heewɓe e goonɗinɓe ɓee ngari njaadiri, kaalti golleeji ɗi ngaɗunoo.
44019019	Boŋobii'en heewɓe ndeentini dewte muuɗum'en, nduppi ɗe yeeso yimɓe fuu. Ɓe kiisii coggu majje, ɓe tawi ana foti ujunaaji capanɗe joy kaalisi daneejo.
44019020	Hono nii, haala Joomiraaɗo kaa ɓeydorii saakaade e heewde semmbe.
44019021	Caggal ɗum, Pool fellisi seekude Makedoniya e Akaya faade Urusaliima. O wii: --So mi tilike ton, waajibi mi yaha Roma duu.
44019022	O neli gollidooɓe makko ɗiɗon, Timote e Erasta, njaha Makedoniya. Kanko, o faɓɓi Asiya.
44019023	E oon wakkati, fitina mawɗo waɗi sabaabu laawol Joomiraaɗo ngol.
44019024	Baylo ndaneeri biyeteeɗo Demeteriyus ana tafa cuuroy kaalisi nanndukoy e rewrudu tooru biyeteeɗo Artemis. Omo heɓa hen tino heewngo, kanko e gollooɓe makko.
44019025	O reentini ɓeen e woɓɓe ɓe nanndi golle, o wii ɗum'en: --Yiɓɓe, oɗon anndi e oo ɗoo golle keɓal meeɗen ngal fawii.
44019026	Oɗon njiya, oɗon nana Pool majjinii yimɓe heewɓe, wanaa ley Efeesu ɗoo tan, ley leyɗe Asiya fuu. O haalani ɓe kulle deweteeɗe ɗe yimɓe moƴƴiniri juuɗe mum'en ɗee nganaa deweteeɗe.
44019027	So jokkii nii, yimɓe mbonnan golle meeɗen. Wanaa ɗum tan, yimɓe ŋoottan teddinde rewrudu Artemis nduu duu, tooru men mawɗo mo hoɗuɓe Asiya e aduna oo fuu ndewata oo.
44019028	Nde ɓe nani ɗiin haalaaji ndee, ɓe mettaa sanne, hedde eɓe ngulla, eɓe mbiya: --Artemis Efeesunkooɓe yo mawɗo! Artemis Efeesunkooɓe yo mawɗo!
44019029	Ngalluure ndee fuu jiiɓii. Gooto fuu dogani boowal manngal ngal. Ɓe ndaasi Gayus e Aristarka Makedoniyankooɓe, yaaduɓe Pool ɓee.
44019030	Pool ana yiɗi naatude hakkunde jamaa oo, kaa taalibaaɓe ɓee kaɗi mo ɗum.
44019031	Yoga e hooreeɓe leydi Asiya, yiɓɓe makko, neli e makko ana ndaarda mo pati o naata boowal too.
44019032	E oon wakkati, jamaa oo ana jiiɓii sanne. Ɓee ana ngullana ɗum ɗoo, ɓee too ana ngullana ɗum gaa. Ko ɓuri heewde e yimɓe ɓee anndaa fay ko hawrintini ɗum'en.
44019033	Yoga e jamaa oo kaaltani haala kaa gorko biyeteeɗo Aleksandere mo Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee ngaɗi kaaloowo muuɗum'en oo. Aleksandere huncani ɓe junngo faa jinngana yimɓe muuɗum ɓee.
44019034	Kaa nde ɓe annditinnoo o Yahuudiyanke ndee, ɓe fuu eɓe ngulla ko waarata e leeruuji ɗiɗi, eɓe mbiya: --Artemis Efeesunkooɓe yo mawɗo!
44019035	Nden binndoowo ngalluure ndee deƴƴini jamaa oo, wii: --Onon Efeesunkooɓe, homo woni mo anndaa ngalluure Efeesu ndee woni hayboore rewrudu Artemis deweteeɗo mawɗo oo, kaɲum e natal muuɗum iwrungal dow kammu ngal?
44019036	Nde wonnoo fay gooto waawaa yeddude ɗum, oɗon kaani jippinde hakkillaaji mooɗon pati ngolliron fay huunde e heɲaare.
44019037	Worɓe ɓe ngaddu-ɗon ɓee, nganaa wujjooɓe kulle rewrudu, nganaa yennooɓe deweteeɗo meeɗen oo.
44019038	So tawii Demeteriyus e gollooɓe wonduɓe e muuɗum ɓee won mo njiɗi wullanaade, ɲalaaɗe careteeɗe ana ndarnaa, kaanankooɓe sarooɓe ana ngoodi, yo ɓe noddondir!
44019039	Kaa so tawii won goɗɗum ko ndaartaton, to deental saahiiɓe ɗum saroytee.
44019040	Eɗen mbaawi felireede murtere waɗunde hannde ndee, sabi fitina baaɗo nii walaa fay daliili gooto.
44019041	Caggal ɗii haalaaji, o firriti jamaa oo.
44020001	Nde fitina oo yawti ndee, Pool mooɓti taalibaaɓe ɓee, waajii ɗum'en. Caggal ɗum, waynii ɗum'en, feewi Makedoniya.
44020002	O seeki ndiin leydi, omo waajoo yimɓe ɓee haalaaji keewɗi. Caggal ɗum, o yehi Yuunan.
44020003	O waɗi ton lebbi tati. O lanndinii faa o naata laana faade Siriya. Kaa caggal nde Yahuudiyankooɓe ndawridi faa njammboo mo, o anniyii wirfitoraade laawol Makedoniya.
44020004	Ɓee ɗoo ɗowtunoo mo: Sopater ɓii Pirrus jeyaaɗo Bereya, e Aristarka e Sekundus jeyaaɓe Tesaloniiki, e Gayus jeyaaɗo Derbe e Timote e Tikikus e Torofim jeyaaɓe leydi Asiya.
44020005	Ɓeen ardii min, ndoomoyi min Torowas.
44020006	Minen, min naati laana faade Filipa caggal iidi mo buuru ƴuufinaaka. E ley balɗe joy min kewtii ɓe Torowas, min ngaɗi ɗon yontere.
44020007	Ɲannde aranndeere e yontere, tawi miɗen mooɓtii faa min taƴa buuru. Pool ana waajoo yimɓe ɓee, nde wonnoo omo anniyii wittude janngo mum. O jokki e waaju oo faa hejjere jemma.
44020008	Lampaaji keewɗi ana ngonnoo e ley suudu dowuuru ndu min mooɓtinoo e muuɗum nduu.
44020009	Suka jokolle biyeteeɗo Ewtikus ana jooɗii dow falanteere. Ko Pool juutini waaju muuɗum oo koo, Ewtikus ɗaanii ɗoyngol teddungol. O saami iwde e falanteere sooro tataɓo ngoo. Nde ɓe ɓamti mo ndee, tawi o maayii.
44020010	Kaa Pool jippii, hippii e makko, ɓami mo e juuɗe muuɗum, wii: --Mbaaltee! Yonki makko wartii e makko!
44020011	Nii Pool ŋabbiti, taƴi buuru, ɲaami. Caggal ɗum, o jokki waaju makko faa weenndoogo, o witti.
44020012	Suka jokolle oo naɓtaa ana wuuri. Ɗum ɓuuɓini ɓerɗe maɓɓe sanne.
44020013	Minen, min adii wirfitaade, min naati laana faade Assos ɗo min kaani naatinde Pool, sabi o anniyiiɗo yaarude ton koyɗe.
44020014	Nde min tawondiri Assos ndee, min naanni mo laana, min peewi Mitilene.
44020015	Min iwi ɗon e laana, min njottoyii janngo mum yeeso ruunde Kiyos. Faɓɓi-janngo mum min ƴaɓɓorii bannge ruunde Samos, faɓɓiti-janngo mum min njottii Miletus.
44020016	Pool fellisii ƴaɓɓoraade Efeesu, sabi o yiɗaa neeptude e leydi Asiya ndii, omo heɲoo yottaade Urusaliima ɲannde iidi Pantekot so tawii ana laatoo.
44020017	Nde Pool wonnoo Miletus ndee, nelani hooreeɓe deental goonɗinɓe Efeesu ɓee.
44020018	Nde ɓe ngari ndee, o wii ɓe: --Oɗon anndi no ngorru-mi e mooɗon gila ɲannde koyngal am adii naatude e leydi Asiya ndii faa hannde.
44020019	Mi golliranii Joomiraaɗo leyɗinkinaare fuu, kaɲum e gonɗi keewɗi e torraaji Yahuudiyankooɓe kewtiiɗi kam ɗii.
44020020	Oɗon anndi mi suuɗaali on huunde fuu ko nafata on, mi waajike on, mi jannginii on hakkunde yimɓe kaɲum e ley galleeji mooɗon.
44020021	Mi tinndinii Yahuudiyankooɓe e Yunaninkooɓe fuu tuubana Laamɗo, ngoonɗina Joomiraaɗo meeɗen Iisaa.
44020022	Jooni, miɗo nii jokki e Ruuhu Ceniiɗo, miɗo yaha Urusaliima, mi anndaa ko hewtoytoo kam ton,
44020023	so wanaa ko Ruuhu Ceniiɗo oo hollata kam: ley geelle ɗee fuu ana wiya kam geƴƴelle e torra ana ndoomi kam.
44020024	Kaa miin, mi jataaki nguurndam am e maayde am fuu so mi heɓii yottinirde golle mo Iisaa Joomiraaɗo halfini kam oo seyo. Oon golle woni seettaade Kabaaru Lobbo haala hinnee Laamɗo.
44020025	Jooni, miɗo anndi on njiitataa kam kasen, onon ɓe ngondunoo-mi so miɗo waajoo ɗum'en haala Laamu Laamɗo oo ɓee.
44020026	Ɗum waɗi so miɗo seettanoo on hannde ɗum ɗoo: so tawii gooto e mooɗon halkiima, wanaa sabaabu am.
44020027	Sabi mi waajike on anniyaaji Laamɗo fuu, mi suuɗaali on fay huunde.
44020028	Ndeenee ko'e mooɗon, ndeenon sewre nde Ruuhu Ceniiɗo oo ɗaldi on ndee, laato-ɗon durooɓe deental goonɗinɓe Laamɗo ngal, sabi ƴiiƴam makko o soottitorii ngal.
44020029	Miin, miɗo anndi caggal am yimɓe bonɓe cooroto e ley mooɗon hono no pobbi nii, kasen duu ɗi njokkan e sewre ndee.
44020030	Fay e ley mooɗon daɲan worɓe immiiɓe ana mbaajoo waajuuji peneeji faa pooɗa taalibaaɓe ɓee njokka caggal muuɗum'en.
44020031	Ɗum nee, njeertee! Miccito-ɗon duuɓi tati, jemma e ɲalooma, mi ŋoottaali waajoraade gooto e mooɗon fuu gonɗi.
44020032	Jooni, mi halfinii on Laamɗo, kaɲum e konngol hinnee muuɗum baawngol naɓude on yeeso e ley goonɗinal, hokka on ko resani sennaaɓe ɓee fuu.
44020033	Abada mi muuyaali fay huunde e mon, wanaa kaalisi, wanaa kaŋŋe, wanaa kaddule.
44020034	Onon e ko'e mooɗon, oɗon anndi juuɗe am ɗee kumti haajuuji am e haajuuji wonduɓe am.
44020035	Mi hollii on e kabaaruuji ɗii fuu, kinaa ngolliron non, mballon lo'uɓe tawa oɗon miccitoo ɗii ɗoo haalaaji ɗi Joomiraaɗo men Iisaa haali kaɲum e hoore muuɗum: "Hokkude ɓuri mbelko'aaku diina hokkoreede."
44020036	Nde Pool tilinoo haalde ɗum ndee, kaɲum e maɓɓe fuu ɓe ndiccii, ɓe nduwii.
44020037	Ɓe fuu ɓe mboyi bojji mawɗi, ɓe kippii e Pool, ɓe caɓɓindii ɗum.
44020038	Ko ɓeydi suŋlinde ɓe ko o wii ɓe njiitataa mo kasen koo. Caggal ɗum, ɓe liwndii mo faa to laana too.
44021001	Nde min ceerti e maɓɓe ndee, min naati laana geeci, min peewi ruunde Kos. Janngo mum, min njottii ruunde Rodusa, min iwi ɗon, min peewi ngeenndi Patara.
44021002	Min keɓi laana lummboowa yaade Finikiya, min naati hen, min ɓettii.
44021003	Nde min njahunoo faa min coynorii Kiprus bannge amen nano, min peewi Siriya, min njottoyii Tirus. Ɗon laana kaa jippinta kaaki muuɗum.
44021004	Min tawi ɗon taalibaaɓe, min ngoni ɗon balɗe jeɗɗi. Eɓe mbiira Pool ley Ruuhu Ceniiɗo pati ŋabbita Urusaliima.
44021005	Nde yontere ndee hiɓɓunoo ndee, min mbitti. Ɓe fuu ɓe liwndii min faa min njalti ngeenndi ndii, kamɓe e rewɓe e sukaaɓe. Min ndiccii dow fonngo maayo geeci, min nduwii.
44021006	Nde min mbaynondirnoo ndee, minen min naati laana, kamɓe ɓe mbirfitii cuuɗi maɓɓe.
44021007	Nde min naati laana Tirus ndee, min njottoyii Potolemayis. Min njowti sakiraaɓe, min ɲallani ɓe, min mbaali.
44021008	Janngo mum, min ndawi, min njottii Kaysariya, min naati suudu Filipa baajotooɗo Kabaaru Lobbo oo, min njippanii ɗum. Kanko omo jeyaa e njeɗɗon suɓaaɓe Urusaliima ɓee.
44021009	Omo jogii ɓiɓɓe rewɓe nayon ɓe ɓamaaka, haaltooɓe ko Laamɗo loowi e mum'en koo.
44021010	Nde min paɓɓunoo ɗon ndee, gorko loowaaɗo konngol Laamɗo biyeteeɗo Agabus iwri Yahuudiya.
44021011	O wari e amen, o ɓami kumorgol Pool, o haɓɓi juuɗe makko e koyɗe makko, o wii: --Ruuhu Ceniiɗo wii: nii Yahuudiyankooɓe wonɓe Urusaliima ɓee kaɓɓirta jeyɗo ngol kumorgol oo, ngaɗa ɗum e juuɗe heeferɓe.
44021012	Nde min nani ɗum ndee, minen e jeyaaɓe ɗon ɓee fuu, min ndaardi Pool pati ŋabba Urusaliima.
44021013	Pool jaabii, wii: --Koɗum waɗi so oɗon mboya, oɗon taƴa ɓernde am? Miin, miɗo lanndinanii ko wanaa haɓɓeede tan, miɗo lanndinanii fay maayde Urusaliima saabe innde Iisaa Joomiraaɗo oo.
44021014	Nde min ndonkunoo waylitinde mo ndee, min celi e makko, min mbii: --Yo muuyɗe Joomiraaɗo laato!
44021015	Caggal ɗeen balɗe, min lanndinii, min ŋabbiti Urusaliima.
44021016	Yoga e taalibaaɓe Kaysariyankooɓe njaadi e amen, naɓi min galle gorko biyeteeɗo Manason, jeyaaɗo Kiprus, laatiiɗo taalibbo gila ko ɓooyi, yalla miɗen jippanoo ɗum.
44021017	Nde min njottii Urusaliima ndee, sakiraaɓe ɓee njaɓɓorii min weltaare.
44021018	Janngo mum, min njaadi e Pool to Yaakuuba. Hooreeɓe deental goonɗinɓe ɓee fuu ana tawanoo ton.
44021019	Caggal ko o jowti ɓe koo, o haalani ɓe huunde fuu ko Laamɗo waɗani yimɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe saabe golle makko.
44021020	Nde ɓe nani ɗum ndee, ɓe njetti Laamɗo. Ɓe mbii Pool: --Sakiike, hono foti ujunaaji Yahuudiyankooɓe njii-ɗaa ko ngoonɗini, haya faa hannde eɓe tiinnii e jokkude Sariya Muusaa oo.
44021021	Ɓe kaalanaama aɗa janngina Yahuudiyankooɓe wonɓe hakkunde leɲi goɗɗi njoppa Sariya Muusaa, mbii-ɗaa pati taada sukaaɓe muuɗum'en kasen, pati njokka neesuuji ɗii kasen.
44021022	Ndennoo, hono ngaɗaten? Sabi min taƴorii ɓe nanan a warii.
44021023	Waɗu ko min kaalante koo. Miɗen njogii ɗoo worɓe nayon ɓamanɓe Laamɗo fodoore.
44021024	Naɓu ɓe cennidaa hoore maa e maɓɓe, njoɓaa ko ɓe kaani yoɓude koo, yalla eɓe mbaawa laɓeede. Yimɓe fuu anndan ko haaletenoo e maa koo fuu wanaa goonga, ɓe anndan kasen aan e hoore maa, aɗa jokki Sariya Muusaa.
44021025	Goonɗinɓe iwɓe e leɲi goɗɗi ɓee, min mbinndii e mum'en ndeentoo e ko hirsanaa tooruuji e ƴiiƴam e jiibuɗi, kaɲum e jeenu.
44021026	Pool ɓami naɓi worɓe ɓee, yaadi e mum'en. Janngo mum, ɓe cennidaa. O naati Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, o haalani yottinooɓe sadaka ɲalaaɗe sennugol ɗee kiɓɓii, faa gooto e maɓɓe fuu waɗanee sadaka.
44021027	Nde balɗe jeɗɗi ɗee ɓadinoo hiɓɓude ndee, yoga e Yahuudiyankooɓe leydi Asiya njii Pool e ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, ɓe njirkiti yimɓe ɓee fuu, ɓe nanngi mo.
44021028	Eɓe ngulla, eɓe mbiya: --Israa'iilankooɓe, paabee min! Oo woni gorko jannginoowo yimɓe e ley nokkuuje ɗee fuu ana bekkisoo yimɓe leɲol meeɗen, ana bekkisoo sariya meeɗen oo, ana bekkisoo nokku ceniiɗo oo. Jooni kaa, o waddii fay Yunaninkooɓe e ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu. O soɓinii oo nokku ceniiɗo!
44021029	Walaa ko ɓe mbiiri non so wanaa ɓe njiino Torofim Efeesunke oo ana wondi e Pool ley ngalluure ndee. Ɓe cikkiino Pool naanniino mo e ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu.
44021030	Jirkitagol ngol huuɓi ngalluure ndee. Yimɓe ana njaltira tatteeji ɗii fuu. Ɓe nanngi Pool, ɓe ndaasi ɗum faa ɓe njaltini ɗum Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, ɓe uddi dame ɗee oon wakkati fuu.
44021031	Nde ɓe tewti faa ɓe mbara Pool ndee, tawi hooreejo sordaasi'en oo humpitike Urusaliima fuu ana darorii koyngal gootal.
44021032	Ɗon e ɗon, o ɓami sordaasi'en e mawɓe muuɗum'en, o dogani ɓe. Nde yimɓe ɓee njii mo kanko e sordaasi'en ɓee ndee, ŋootti fiide Pool.
44021033	O ɓattii Pool, o yamiri Pool nanngee, o wii haɓɓiree calali ɗiɗi, o lamndii kaɲum yo homo e koɗum waɗi?
44021034	Jamaa oo ana wulla. Ɓee ana ngulla geɗel, ɓee too ana ngulla gonngel. Nde wonnoo jirkitaare ndee haɗii mo faamde, o yamiri Pool naɓee to huɓeere too.
44021035	Nde Pool wari faa ŋabba kalikali huɓeere oo ndee, sordaasi'en ɓee ndoondii mo saabe jirkitaare jamaa oo,
44021036	sabi yimɓe heewɓe ana njokki e makko ana ngulla, ana mbiya: --War mo!
44021037	Nde ɓe ngari faa ɓe naanna mo e damal huɓeere ngal ndee, Pool wii hooreejo oo: --Ana daganoo kam mi haalda e maa naa? Oon wii mo: --Ee? Aɗa waawi yunaninkoore naa?
44021038	Ndennoo wanaa aan woni Misiranke gaɗuɗo murtere ko ɓooyaali, wardi e warooɓe ko'e ujunaaji nayon, naɓi ɗum'en ley ladde jeereende oo?
44021039	Pool jaabii, wii: --Miin, mi Yahuudiyanke pinɗo Tarsus ley leydi Silisi, e ndee ngalluure nde wanaa ɲooɓunde njeyaa-mi. Miɗo ɲaage nduŋano-ɗaa kam mi haalda e yimɓe ɓee.
44021040	O duŋanii ɗum. Pool darii e dow ŋabbirde ndee, huncani yimɓe ɓee junngo. Nde ɓe ndeƴƴininoo ndee, o haali e ibaraninkoore, o wii:
44022001	--Sakiraaɓe e baabiraaɓe, kettinee jooni faa mi fammina on mi waɗaali ko boni.
44022002	Nde ɓe nani ibaraninkoore o haaldata e maɓɓe ndee, ɓe ndeƴƴinii teen. O wii:
44022003	--Mi Yahuudiyanke pinɗo Tarsus ley leydi Silisi. Kaa ɗo Urusaliima ɗoo mawnu-mi. Gamaliyel wonnoo moobbo am. Kanko janngini kam sariya njaatiraaɓe meeɗen oo faa paamu-mi. Miɗo jootunoo e Laamɗo hono no on fuu ngorru-ɗon hannde nii.
44022004	Mi torrii jokkuɓe ngol ɗoo Laawol ɓee faa maayi. Mi nanngii worɓe e rewɓe, mi uddii ɗum'en kasu.
44022005	Jottinoowo Sadaka Mawɗo e waalde Saahiiɓe ɓee fuu ana ceettanoo kam kaɲum'en duu. Keɓu-mi e maɓɓe kasen talki faa mi holla sakiraaɓe maɓɓe wonɓe Damas ɓee, njaa-mi haɓɓoyde jokkuɓe laawol Iisaa wonɓe ton ɓee, faa mi wadda ɗum'en Urusaliima yalla ana caree.
44022006	Njaa-mi faa ɓadii-mi Damas, wakkati hakkunde naange, fooyre mawnde iwi dow kammu, yaayni, filii kam.
44022007	Caamu-mi e leydi, nan-mi daande ana wiya kam: "Sool, Sool, ko saabii so aɗa torra kam?"
44022008	Njaabii-mi, mbii-mi: "Aan homo, giɗo Laamɗo?" O wii kam: "Miin, Iisaa Nasaraatunke mo torru-ɗaa oo."
44022009	Wonduɓe e am ɓee njii fooyre ndee, kaa ɓe nanaali daande kaalduɗo e am oo.
44022010	Nden, mbii-mi: "Joomiraaɗo, koɗum ngaɗan-mi?" Joomiraaɗo wii kam: "Imma, yaa Damas, a haalante ton ko njamire-ɗaa ngaɗaa koo fuu."
44022011	Wonduɓe e am ɓee ɗowi kam faa ley Damas, sabi fooyre ndee wumniino kam no nde sattiri yaaynude.
44022012	Ananiyas yo gorko kulɗo Laamɗo, jokkuɗo Sariya Muusaa, mo Yahuudiyankooɓe hoɗuɓe ton fuu ceettii moƴƴo oo,
44022013	wari, darii yeeso am, wii kam: "Sool, sakiike, wumtu!" Ɗon e ɗon njii-moo-mi.
44022014	O wii: "Laamɗo njaatiraaɓe meeɗen oo suɓike ma yalla aɗa annda sago muuɗum, njiyaa Pooccitiiɗo oo, nanaa haala muuɗum.
44022015	Sabi aan seettantoo mo yeeso yimɓe fuu ko njii-ɗaa e ko nan-ɗaa.
44022016	Jooni, koɗum ndoomataa? Imma, loote-ɗaa lootogal batisima, njaafire-ɗaa luutti maa e noddude innde Joomiraaɗo."
44022017	Caggal mi wirfitike Urusaliima, miɗo rewa Laamɗo ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, faa won ko ƴellitii e am,
44022018	nden njii-mi Joomiraaɗo, wii kam: "Heɲa law, yaltu Urusaliima, sabi ɓe njaɓataa seedaaku mo ceettanto-ɗaa kam oo."
44022019	Njaabii-mi, mbii-mi: "Joomiraaɗo, eɓe anndi miɗo yahannoo ley cuuɗi baajorɗi ɗii fuu, miɗo uddannoo miɗo fiyannoo goonɗinɓe ma ɓee.
44022020	Nde ƴiiƴam Eciyen seede maa oo yuppetee ndee, miɗo darii, eɗum weli kam ko o waraa koo, miin haybannoo kaddule warɓe mo ɓee."
44022021	Joomiraaɗo jaabii kam, wii: "Yaa, mi nelete to woɗɗi to yimɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe."
44022022	Eɓe kettinanii mo faa o haali ngol konngol. Nden ɓe ngulli, ɓe mbii: --Ittu mo e leydi ndii! Hono oo haanaa wuurde!
44022023	Eɓe ngulla, eɓe mbeeynaa saayaaji maɓɓe, eɓe immina colla.
44022024	Hooreejo oo yamiri Pool naɓee to ley huɓeere too, lamndoree piiɗe faa ɓe annda ko saabii so jamaa oo ana wulla e makko hono nii.
44022025	Nde ɓe kaɓɓi mo faa ɓe piya mo ndee, o wii mawɗo gonɗo ɗon oo: --Ana daganoo on piyon Romanke sako mo saraaka naa?
44022026	Nde mawɗo oo nani ɗum ndee, haalanoyi hooreejo oo, wii: --Aɗa anndi ko kosu-ɗaa faa ngaɗaa naa? Gorko oo yo Romanke non!
44022027	Nden hooreejo oo yehi to Pool, lamndii ɗum, wii: --Haalanam, soobee fuu a Romanke naa? Pool jaabii, wii: --Kaɲum!
44022028	Hooreejo oo jaabii, wii: --Miin, so wanaa njoɓu-mi kaalisi keewɗo nde keɓu-mi laataade Romanke. Pool wii mo: --Miin, mi finii mi tawii mi kaɲum.
44022029	Ɗon e ɗon anniyiiɓe fiide mo faa tilsina mo haaltude ɓee njalti. Hooreejo oo huli, sabi anndii Pool yo Romanke, haɓɓiino ɗum.
44022030	Janngo mum, kammari hooreejo oo ana yiɗunoo taƴorde ko Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee ngullanirii Pool, humti ɗum, yamiri hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka e waalde Saahiiɓe ndee fuu kawrita. Caggal ɗum, o waddi Pool, o darni ɗum yeeso maɓɓe.
44023001	Pool ƴeewi waalde Saahiiɓe ɓee, wii: --Sakiraaɓe, hakkille baaltiiɗo nguurdu-mi yeeso Joomiraaɗo gila pinu-mi faa yottaade ɲalooma hannde oo.
44023002	Nii Ananiyas, Jottinoowo Sadaka Mawɗo oo, yamiri darinooɓe bannge makko ɓee piya mo e hunduko.
44023003	Nden, Pool wii mo: --Laamɗo fiyete, aan kokowol dawninaangol! A jooɗoto faa cariraa kam Sariya Muusaa, ko njamir-ɗaa mi fiyee koo a luuttii Sariya Muusaa.
44023004	Darinooɓe ɗon ɓee mbii Pool: --A yennan Jottinoowo Sadaka Mawɗo mo Laamɗo suɓii oo naa?
44023005	Pool jaabii, wii: --Sakiraaɓe, mi anndaa o Jottinoowo Sadaka Mawɗo, sabi miɗo anndi ana winndii: "Pati yennu hooreejo leɲol maa!"
44023006	Nde wonnoo Pool ana anndi yoga e Saahiiɓe ɓee yo Saduki'en, yoga mum'en yo Farisa'en, duki semmbe, wii: --Sakiraaɓe, miin mi Farisanke, ɓii Farisanke. Saabe fawgol jikke e immital maayɓe carirtee-mi.
44023007	Nde o haalnoo ɗum ndee, Farisa'en ɓee e Saduki'en ɓee njeddondiri, deental ngal feccii.
44023008	Tawi Saduki'en ana mbiya immital walaa, malaa'ika'en ngalaa, ruuhuuji ngalaa, kaa Farisa'en ana ngoonɗini ɗum fuu.
44023009	Duko ngoo ɓeydii mawnude. Yoga e dunkee'en Sariya heedanɓe Farisa'en ɓee ndarii, immini duko manngo, ana mbiya: --Walaa fuu ko boni ko min njii e oo gorko. Ana waawi taweede ruuhu naa malaa'ika haaldi e makko!
44023010	Jeddi ɗii mawni faa hooreejo sordaasi'en oo huli pati Pool seekee. Ɗum waɗi so o yamiri sordaasi'en njippoo to deental too, itta Pool e juuɗe yimɓe ɓee, naɓta ɗum to huɓeere too.
44023011	Jemma jokkuɗo hen oo, Joomiraaɗo darii yeeso Pool, wii ɗum: --Pati hul! No ceettanori-ɗaa kam ley Urusaliima nii, ana haani ceettanoro-ɗaa kam non Roma duu.
44023012	Nde weetunoo ndee, Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee ngaɗi gaddal, kunii ɲaamataa njarataa gila ɗoo faa mbara Pool.
44023013	Wannooɓe ngal gaddal ɓee ana ɓuri capanɗe nayon gorko.
44023014	Ɓe njehi to hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka e mawɓe, ɓe mbii: --Min kunike hunoore fay huunde min ɲaamataa min njarataa gila ɗoo faa min mbara Pool.
44023015	Jooni, onon e waalde Saahiiɓe ɓee, mbiyee hooreejo sordaasi'en oo waddana on Pool, mbiyon oɗon njiɗi faamtindaade ko o haalannoo koo. Minen, miɗen lanndinii faa min mbara mo gila mo yottaaki.
44023016	Baaɗii Pool gorko nani haala gaddal ngal, yehi to huɓeere too, naati, humpiti Pool.
44023017	Pool noddi gooto e mawɓe sordaasi'en ɓee, wii ɗum: --Naɓu oo suka gorko to hooreejo too, sabi won ko o yiɗi haalande ɗum.
44023018	Mawɗo sordaasi'en oo naɓi mo to hooreejo muuɗum too, wii ɗum: --Nanngaaɗo biyeteeɗo Pool oo noddi kam, ɲaagii kam mi wadda oo suka gorko to maa, sabi won ko oon yiɗi haalande ma.
44023019	Hooreejo oo nanngi junngo makko, sawdintini mo, wii: --Koɗum kaalantaa kam?
44023020	O wii ɗum: --Yahuudiyankooɓe kaaldii, kawrii, ndaardete janngo yalla aɗa waddana ɗum'en Pool yeeso waalde Saahiiɓe ɓee, ɓe nanndinkinoo e yiɓɓe faamtindaade ko o haalannoo koo.
44023021	Pati njaɓanaa ɓe! Sabi ko ɓuri worɓe capanɗe nayon e maɓɓe ana ɲugganii mo, kunike ɲaamataa njarataa so mbaraali mo. Ɓe lanndinike, eɓe ndoomi yamiroore maa.
44023022	Hooreejo oo wii suka gorko oo: --Pati haalan fay gooto a haalanii kam ɗum. O yoppi ɗum witti.
44023023	Caggal ɗum, o noddi mawɓe sordaasi'en makko ɗiɗon, o wii ɗum'en: --Mooɓtee worɓe teemeɗe ɗiɗon e waɗɗiiɓe pucci capanɗe njeɗɗon, kaɲum e teemeɗe ɗiɗon jom'en gaawe. On fuu, lanndinee yaade Kaysariya wakkati jeenaɓo jemma.
44023024	Kaɓɓee pucci faa naɓiron Pool e dow jam, to Filikus goforneer oo too.
44023025	Hooreejo oo winndi oo ɓataaki:
44023026	Miin, Kalawdiyus Lisiyas, miɗo jowte, aan Filikus goforneer tedduɗo oo.
44023027	Gorko mo neldu-maa-mi oo, Yahuudiyankooɓe nanngunoo ɗum, anniyii warde ɗum. Nde kumpitinoo-mi o Romanke ndee, naatu-mi hen, miin e fedde sordaasi'en ndee, mbiltu-moo-mi.
44023028	Nde wonnoo miɗo yiɗi faamde ko ɓe ngullanirii mo ndee, ngaddu-moo-mi yeeso waalde Saahiiɓe maɓɓe.
44023029	Taw-mi banngal sariya maɓɓe tan ɓe ngullanirii mo, kaa ko o wullanaa e muuɗum koo, waawaa waddande mo wareede naa uddeede.
44023030	Caggal ɗum, martu-mi kumpa Yahuudiyankooɓe ndawridii faa nannga mo. Ɗum waɗi so neldu-maa-mi mo ɗon e ɗon, njamir-mi wullaniiɓe mo ɓee duu njaha to maa.
44023031	Sordaasi'en ɓee ngaɗi ko njamiraa koo, ɓami Pool ley jemmaaku, naɓi ɗum faa Antibatiris.
44023032	Janngo mum, sordaasi'en yaarannooɓe koyɗe ɓee mbirfitii to huɓeere too, ɗaldi Pool waɗɗiiɓe pucci ɓee njottinoya ɗum.
44023033	Nde ɓeen njottinoo Kaysariya ndee, ndokki goforneer oo ɓataaki oo, kolli ɗum Pool.
44023034	Nde kaananke oo janngi ɓataaki oo ndee, lamndii hoto o jeyaa. Nde o nani Silisi Pool jeyaa ndee,
44023035	o wii ɗum: --So wullaniiɓe ma ɓee ngarii, mi nanan haala maa. O yamiri oon mooɓtoyee to suudu laamordu Hirudus too.
44024001	Balɗe joy caggal muuɗum, Ananiyas Jottinoowo Sadaka Mawɗo oo yottii Kaysariya ana wondi e yoga e mawɓe ɓee, kaɲum e dunkee sariya Romankooɓe biyeteeɗo Tartulus. Ɓe ngullanii Pool to goforneer oo.
44024002	Nde Pool noddaa ndee, Tartulus fuɗɗi wullanaade mo yeeso kaananke oo, wii: --Filikus kaananke tedduɗo, laamu maa waddanii min jam ɓooyɗo, kasen ɲeeɲal maa waylitii leɲol ngol sanne.
44024003	Ɗum fuu saabe maa min keɓiri tatteeji fuu, min njettii ma sanne.
44024004	Mi yiɗaa joonnde ndee juuta, kaa miɗo ndaarde saabe moƴƴuki maa, kettinano-ɗaa min seeɗa.
44024005	Min tawii oo ɗoo gorko yo bonɗo sanne, gaddoowo fitina hakkunde Yahuudiyankooɓe wonɓe e aduna oo ɓee fuu. O hooreejo diina Nasaraatunkooɓe oo.
44024006	O naatii e soɓinde Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, ɗum nee min nanngii mo. [
44024007	]
44024008	Aan e hoore maa, lamndo-ɗaa mo, paamaa ko min ngullanirii mo koo fuu.
44024009	Yahuudiyankooɓe tawdaaɓe e makko ɓee mbii non jaati worri.
44024010	Nde goforneer oo hokkunoo Pool haala ndee, jaabii: --Miɗo anndi waɗii duuɓi aɗa sara ngol leɲol. Ɗum waɗi so miɗo seyoroo liddi am ɗii.
44024011	Ɓuraa balɗe sappo e ɗiɗi ko ngar-mi Urusaliima faa mi rewa Laamɗo. So a taykiima, aan e hoore maa, a tawan hono non worri.
44024012	Fay gooto tawaali kam miɗo hiitondira e neɗɗo naa miɗo jirkita jamaa, wanaa e ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, wanaa e ley cuuɗi baajorɗi, wanaa e ley ngalluure ndee.
44024013	Ɓe mbaawaa tabintinde ko ɓe ngullanirii kam e muuɗum jooni koo.
44024014	Kaa miɗo jaɓi yeeso maa: miɗo rewri Laamɗo njaatiraaɓe meeɗen oo diina mo ɓe mbiyata diina peneejo oo. Miɗo goonɗini ko winndaa e Tawreeta Muusaa koo e ko winndaa e dewte annabaaɓe koo fuu.
44024015	Kasen duu miɗo fawi jikke am e Laamɗo mo ɓe pawi jikke maɓɓe e muuɗum kamɓe duu oo, o wuurtinan fooccitiiɓe e ɓe pooccitaaki fuu.
44024016	Ɗum saabii so tiinnitii-mi yalla ana laatanoo kam hakkille baaltiiɗo ɲannde fuu ko waldaa e feloore yeeso Laamɗo e yeeso yimɓe.
44024017	Caggal duuɓi keewɗi, ngartu-mi faa mi waɗana yimɓe am dokke, mi itta sadakaaji.
44024018	E ley majjum ɓe tawi kam e ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu caggal mi sennaama, mi waldaa e jamaa, mi waldaa e dillere.
44024019	Yoga e Yahuudiyankooɓe leydi Asiya wonnooɓe ɗon, ɓeen kaannoo warde wullanaade kam yeeso maa, so tawii won ko ɓe ngullantoo kam.
44024020	Naa ɓee ɗoo, kaɲum e hoore mum'en kaala boofi ɗi njii e am nde ndarinoo-mi yeeso waalde Saahiiɓe ndee,
44024021	so wanaa konngol gootol ngol ndarii-mi so ngullu-mi, mbii-mi: "Saabe immital maayɓe carirton kam hannde!"
44024022	Nde Filikus nannoo ɗum ndee, riiwti ɓe e dow no mo anndiri diina oo. O wii: --So Lisiyas hooreejo oo warii, mi saran haala mooɗon kaa.
44024023	O yamiri mawɗo sordaasi'en oo hayba Pool, waɗana ɗum mosolaa, pati haɗa fay gooto e yiɓɓe muuɗum ɓee gollande ɗum naa warde e muuɗum.
44024024	Balɗe seeɗa caggal muuɗum, Filikus wardi e jom suudu muuɗum Yahuudiyanke biyeteeɗo Durusilla. O neli Pool waddoyee, o nanii ana haala haala goonɗinal Iisaa Almasiihu.
44024025	Kaa nde Pool haalannoo haala fooccitaare e nantaare e sariya garoowo ndee, Filikus huli, wii: --Jooni kaa, gasii, yaa! Nde keɓindii-mi fuu, mi nodditete.
44024026	O miilii Pool hokkan mo kaalisi. Ɗum saabii so omo nodda ɗum cili keewɗi faa ɓe ngaajodoo.
44024027	Kaa nde ɗum heɓunoo duuɓi ɗiɗi ndee, Porsiyus Festus loomtii Filikus, laatii kaananke. Nde wonnoo Filikus ana yiɗi seynude Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee, yoppi Pool e ley kasu oo.
44025001	Balɗe tati caggal ko Festus wari e ley leydi ndii koo, iwi Kaysariya, yehi Urusaliima.
44025002	Ɗon, hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka e mawɓe Yahuudiyankooɓe ngari to makko ngullitanii Pool. Ɓe ndaardi mo soobee
44025003	o hokka ɓe Pool, ɓe ngadda ɗum Urusaliima, sabi eɓe tewta no ɓe njanira mo, ɓe mbara mo.
44025004	Festus wii Pool ana uddii kasu Kaysariya too, kanko e hoore makko o birfitotooɗo ton law.
44025005	O wii: --Mawɓe mooɗon ngara njaada e am Kaysariya, ngullanoo gorko oo so tawii won ko waɗi.
44025006	Festus faɓɓidaali e maɓɓe ko ɓuri balɗe jetti naa sappo, caggal ɗum, o regii o feewi Kaysariya. Janngo mum, o jooɗoyii to sarirde too, o yamiri Pool waddee.
44025007	Nde Pool yottii ndee, Yahuudiyankooɓe iwɓe Urusaliima ɓee pilii ɗum, kappi ɗum kuɗɗe bonɗe keewɗe, ɗe ngalaa daliili.
44025008	Pool jaabii, ana wiya: --Mi meeɗaali tooɲude, wanaa sariya Yahuudiyankooɓe oo, wanaa Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, wanaa kaananke Roma mawɗo oo.
44025009	Nde wonnoo Festus ana yiɗi seynude Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee, lamndii Pool, wii: --Aɗa jaɓa yaade Urusaliima faa miin e hoore am mi saroya ton kabaaru maa oo naa?
44025010	Pool wii: --E sarirde kaananke Roma mawɗo ngon-mi, ɗo kaan-mi sareede ɗoo. Mi tooɲaali Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee, no aan e hoore maa anndir-ɗaa ɗum nii.
44025011	So tawii miin tooɲi, mi waɗii ko foti warde kam, mi salataako wareede. Kaa so fay huunde e ko ɓe kappi kam koo wanaa goonga, fay gooto waawaa wattude kam e juuɗe maɓɓe. Sariya am ɓettinee, yaha to kaananke Roma mawɗo oo.
44025012	Caggal nde Festus haaldi e howruuɓe muuɗum, jaabii, wii: --Sariya maa ɓettinee to kaananke Roma mawɗo njiɗ-ɗaa, ɗum nee, a ɓettinte yaade to kaananke Roma mawɗo!
44025013	Balɗe seeɗa caggal muuɗum, Agirippa kaananke oo e Barniki ngari Kaysariya jowtude Festus.
44025014	Nde ɓe paɓɓunoo ɗon balɗe seeɗa ndee, Festus haalani kaananke oo haala Pool, wii: --Won gorko mo Filikus yoppi ɗoo e kasu.
44025015	Nde njaa-mi Urusaliima ndee, hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka e mawɓe Yahuudiyankooɓe kaalanii kam haala makko, ɲaagiima mi sara mo.
44025016	Njaabii-mi ɓe: Romankooɓe neesoraaki sarde neɗɗo tawee jooddaaki e happuɓe ɗum ɓee, jaaboo ɗum'en.
44025017	Nde ɓe mooɓtinoo so ɓe ngari ɗoo ndee, miin nee, mi neemtinaali fay huunde. Janngo mum, njooɗoyii-mi to sarirde too, njamir-mi gorko oo waddee.
44025018	Nde wullaniiɓe mo ɓee ndarii bannge makko ndee, ngaddaali fay feloore wootere e ko miilannoo-mi koo.
44025019	Ɓe ngaddi e makko haalaaji banngal diina maɓɓe, kaɲum e gooto biyeteeɗo Iisaa maayɗo, mo Pool wiyata ana wuuri oo.
44025020	Miin nii, haala wa'uka nii ana wemmbi kam, ɗum waɗi so lamndi-moo-mi yalla omo jaɓa saroyeede Urusaliima naa?
44025021	Kaa o ɲaagiima kabaaru makko wattee e juuɗe kaananke mawɗo oo, ndennoo njamir-mi o haybee ɗoo faa mi heɓa neldude mo kaananke Roma mawɗo oo.
44025022	Agirippa wii Festus: --Miɗo yiɗi hettinaade oo gorko, miin e hoore am. Festus wii: --A hettinto mo janngo.
44025023	Janngo mum, Agirippa e Barniki ngardi e fuukinaare mawnde, naati e ley sarirdu nduu, kamɓe e hooreeɓe sordaasi'en ɓee e mawɓe ngalluure ndee. Festus yamiri Pool waddee.
44025024	Festus wii: --Agirippa kaananke e deental tawaaɓe ɗoo! On njii oo gorko. Yahuudiyankooɓe fuu ngullanike mo ga am ley Urusaliima e ɗoo fuu, eɓe ngulla eɓe mbiya o haanaa yoppeede o wuura.
44025025	Miin e hoore am, mi tawii o waɗaali fay huunde ko haani warde mo. Kaa nde wonnoo kanko e hoore makko o ɲaagiima sariya makko ɓettinee, naɓee to kaananke Roma mawɗo oo, mi fellisii neldude mo ton.
44025026	Mi walaa taƴoral fuu e makko ko kaan-mi winndude e kaananke oo. Ɗum waɗi so ndarnu-moo-mi yeeso mooɗon on fuu, faa ɗum teeŋa e maa, aan Agirippa kaananke oo, yalla so en kettinike haala makko, miɗo heɓa ko mi winnda.
44025027	Sabi ɗum gasataa no kasunke neldirtee kaananke mawɗo oo tawee ko nanngiraa koo hollitaaka faa laaɓa.
44026001	Agirippa wii Pool: --A hokkaama haala, haal haala maa. Nden, Pool hunci junngo, jaabii, wii:
44026002	--Agirippa kaananke, mi seyorike hujjaade yeeso maa hannde ko Yahuudiyankooɓe ngullanirii kam koo fuu.
44026003	Sabi aɗa anndi neesuuji Yahuudiyankooɓe e haalaaji muuɗum'en fuu. Saabe majjum miɗo ɲaage, muɲaa, kettinano-ɗaa kam.
44026004	Yahuudiyankooɓe fuu ana anndi no nguurdu-mi gila mi cukalel tusukel. Eɓe anndi no ngorrunoo-mi e ley suudu baaba am e ley Urusaliima fuu.
44026005	Eɓe anndi gila arannde, so ɓe njaɓii seettaade: miɗo jokki laawol diina amen ɓurngol tiiɗude ngol, miɗo hiisodaa e Farisa'en.
44026006	Jooni, mi darike faa mi saree saabe mi fawii jikke am dow fodoore nde Laamɗo waɗani njaatiraaɓe meeɗen ndee.
44026007	Leɲi meeɗen sappo e ɗiɗi ɗii ana pawi jikke muuɗum e tabital fodoore ndee, ana ndewira soobee jemma e ɲalooma. Kaananke, saabe oo jikke Yahuudiyankooɓe ngullanorii kam!
44026008	Ko saabii so onon Yahuudiyankooɓe miil-ɗon Laamɗo waawaa immitinde maayɓe?
44026009	Miin e hoore am, e ɓettaade mi taƴoriino miɗo haani bonnude innde Iisaa Nasaraatunke oo, no laatorii fuu.
44026010	Ɗum woni ko ngaɗu-mi Urusaliima. Hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka ɓee njarraninoo kam mi udda seniiɓe heewɓe e kasu. Nde ɓe caranoo ɓe wareteeɓe ndee, miɗo yarrii ɗum.
44026011	Mi torrii ɓe cili keewɗi e cuuɗi baajorɗi ɗii fuu, mi tilsinii ɓe mbonkoo Joomiraaɗo. Torra am e maɓɓe ana mawnunoo sanne faa miɗo tawoyannoo ɓe ley geelle janane.
44026012	Hono non njaaru-mi Damas nde hooreeɓe yottinooɓe sadaka ɓee njarranii kam ndee.
44026013	Kaananke, miɗo e laawol wakkati hakkunde naange, njii-mi fooyre ana iwa dow kammu ana filoo kam, miin e yaaduɓe e am ɓee fuu. Fooyre ndee ana ɓuri naange jalbude.
44026014	Min fuu, min caami e leydi, nan-mi daande ana wiya kam e ley ibaraninkoore: "Sool, Sool, ko saabii so aɗa torra kam? So ndemoori wii saloto ko nannguɗo ginol mum waɗata fuu, ɓeydan naawnaade."
44026015	Njaabii-mi, mbii-mi: "Aan homo, giɗo Laamɗo?" Joomiraaɗo wii: "Miin, Iisaa mo torru-ɗaa oo.
44026016	Imma dara, sabi mi ɓannganii ma mi suɓike ma faa ngollanaa kam, ceedano-ɗaa kam ley ko njii-ɗaa koo e ko anniyii-mi ɓannginanoyde ma caggal hannde.
44026017	Mi reenete e Yahuudiyankooɓe e yimɓe leɲi goɗɗi, ɓe nelan-maa-mi e muuɗum jooni ɓee,
44026018	yalla aɗa feerta gite maɓɓe, ɓe iwa e nimre, ɓe ngarta e fooyre, ɓe iwa e junngo Ibiliisa, ɓe ngarta e Laamɗo, ɓe keɓa yaafeede luutti, ɓe ndonida e sennaaɓe ɓee saabe ko ɓe goonɗini kam koo."
44026019	Kaananke Agirippa, ɗum waɗi so mi salaaki ɗowtanaade ko njii-mi, ko iwrani kam dow kammu koo.
44026020	Ɓe miɗo adoo waajaade fuu yo yimɓe Damas e yimɓe Urusaliima e piilol Yahuudiya fuu. Caggal ɗum, njokkin-mi hen yimɓe leɲi goɗɗi tuuba, ngarta e Laamɗo, ngolla golleeji kollitooji ɓe tuubii.
44026021	Saabe ɗum Yahuudiyankooɓe nanngiri kam ley Suudu Dewal Mawndu nduu, tewti warde kam.
44026022	Kaa faa hannde, Laamɗo ana reeni kam. Miɗo seettanoo tedduɓe e lo'uɓe. Mi waajataako fay huunde so wanaa ko annabaaɓe e Sariya Muusaa kaali waroyan koo:
44026023	Almasiihu torroto, adoo maayɓe immitaade. Caggal ɗum, o waajoto fooyre, ko wanaa yimɓe meeɗen tan, o waajoto leɲi goɗɗi duu.
44026024	Nde Pool haalata ɗum ndee, Festus jahii jahaango manngo, wii: --Pool, a haanɗii! Heewgol maa anndal ngol haanɗinii ma!
44026025	Pool jaabii, wii: --Tedduɗo, mi haanɗaali. Ko kaalan-mi koo yo haalaaji goonɗuɗi, jogiiɗi maanaa.
44026026	Agirippa kaananke oo ana anndi kuɗɗe ɗee. Ɗum waɗi so miɗo hoolii haalde ɗum yeeso makko. Sabi miɗo taƴori fay huunde ɲooɓanaali mo hen, sabi ɗum waɗaali e cuucuukka.
44026027	Kaananke! Aɗa goonɗini annabaaɓe naa? Miɗo anndi aɗa goonɗini!
44026028	Agirippa wii Pool: --Seeɗa tan haɗete waɗude kam neɗɗo Iisaa.
44026029	Pool jaabii, wii: --Yaawi taaɗi fuu, mi ɲaagoto Laamɗo faa aan e hettintooɓe kam jooni ɓee fuu laato-ɗon ko ngon-mi koo, tawee ɓoggol e calali ngalaa e mon.
44026030	Kaananke oo e goforneer oo e Barniki e jooddinooɓe e muuɗum'en ɓee fuu immii.
44026031	Nde ɓe njalti suudu nduu ndee, eɓe mbiyondira: --O waɗaali ko haani warde mo naa ko haani uddude mo kasu.
44026032	Agirippa wii Festus: --Omo waawnoo yoppiteede so o wiyaalino sariya makko ɓettinee naɓee to kaananke Roma mawɗo oo.
44027001	Nde yaarugol amen Italiya laana tabitinnoo ndee, Pool e kasunkooɓe woɓɓe ngaɗaa e junngo mawɗo sordaasi'en biyeteeɗo Yuliyus, jeyaaɗo e fedde sordaasi'en kaananke Roma mawɗo oo.
44027002	Min naati laana geeci iwka Adaramatiya njahoowa so ana faŋa ley leydi Asiya, min ndeerti. Miɗen ngondi e Aristarka gorko Makedoniyanke iwoowo Tesaloniiki.
44027003	Janngo mum, min njottii Sidon. Yuliyus waɗani Pool mosolaa, duŋanii ɗum yaha to yiɓɓe mum yalla ana paaboroo ɗum ko hasindini e mum.
44027004	Nde min iwi ɗon ndee, min ɓattitii fonngo ruunde Kiprus, sabi e henndu min peewtunoo.
44027005	Min lummbiri maayo geeci ngoo hedde Silisi e Pamfiliya, min njottii Mira ley leydi Lisiya.
44027006	Ɗon, mawɗo sordaasi'en oo heɓani min laana iwka Aleksandiri ana fa'i Italiya, naanni min hen.
44027007	Balɗe kuurɗe laana amen kaa waɗi ana yaara seese. Semmbe e doole min njottorii daŋŋeere Kinidus. Nde wonnoo henndu nduu haɗii min yawtude ndee, min lummbiri Salmone. Gila ɗon min takkii e fonngo ruunde Kereta.
44027008	Nde min ƴaɓɓorinoo ɗon semmbe e doole ndee, min ngari e nokku biyeteeɗo Hoɗorde Lobbere nde woɗɗaa e ngeenndi Lasiya.
44027009	Nde wonnoo min paɓɓii sanne ndee, dawirde laana geeci hulɓiniima sabi ɲannde hooreteende ɓettike, jaangol ngol duu fuɗɗii. Pool ana jeertina ɓe,
44027010	ana wiya: --Sakiraaɓe, mi yii ngol ɗoo dawol yo keewoowol kunkooji e mursee, wanaa laana kaa e kaaki ɗii tan, ana waawi laataade yonkiiji men duu.
44027011	Kaa mawɗo sordaasi'en oo, haala mawɗo laana oo kaɲum e joomiika ɓuri hoolaade, diina ko Pool haali koo.
44027012	Daŋŋeere nde ɓe ngoni e muuɗum ndee, welaa dabbunde, ɗum waɗi so ɓurɓe heewde e wonɓe e laana ɓee mbii ɓe njaha ɓe tewta yottaade Feniksa, daŋŋeere Kereta fewtunde e soɓɓundu hiirnaange ɓaleeri e soɓɓundu hiirnaange saahal, yalla eɓe ndabba ton.
44027013	Nde henndu iwrundu ɓaleeri fuɗɗi mooyde ndee, ɓe cikki ɓe mbaawan yottinde faandaare maɓɓe ndee. Ɓe ŋabbini torooje ɗee, ɓe takkii e fonngo Kereta, ɓe mbirfitii.
44027014	Kaa caggal ɗum seeɗa, henndu mawndu wiyeteendu henndu funnaange saahal iwri to ruunde too, jippii.
44027015	Laana kaa hayti, min ndonki haɗude henndu nduu naɓude ka. Ɗum waɗi so min acci ka doya.
44027016	Nde min ɓettotoo duungel tusukel biyeteengel Kawda ndee, duungel ngel huuri min seeɗa e henndu, min cippiri ɗon e laanawel tusukel ngel, min kewti ngel.
44027017	Nde ɓe ɓamtunoo ngel ndee, ɓe ɓami ɓoggi, ɓe cacci e laana mawka kaa. Ko ɓe kuli pati ɓe njanoy e soɓɓundu Sirta koo, ɓe jippini wiir oo, ɓe njoppi eka doya.
44027018	Henndu nduu wibbi semmbe. Ɗum waɗi so janngo mum ɓe puɗɗi tippaade donngal laana kaa.
44027019	E ɲalooma tataɓo oo, ɓe mbedorii juuɗe maɓɓe kaaki laana ɗii.
44027020	Balɗe kuurɗe naange e koode fuu njiyataake. No henndu nduu foti mawnude, min taƴi jikke amen fuu e hisude.
44027021	Nde wonnoo yimɓe ɓee paɓɓii keɓaali ko ɲaama, Pool darii hakkunde maɓɓe, wii: --So on njaɓiino haala am on iwaalino Kereta, ɗii kunkooji e oo mursee hewtataakono en.
44027022	Jooni, miɗo haalana on: ceyee, sabi fay gooto e mooɗon yonki muuɗum mursataake, laana kaa tan mursetee.
44027023	Jemma hanken, malaa'ika iwrii to Laamɗo mo ndewan-mi oo warii e am,
44027024	wii kam: "Pool, pati hul, a daroto yeeso kaananke Roma mawɗo oo, Laamɗo reenete aan e dawduɓe e maa ɓee fuu."
44027025	Ndennoo, tiinnee, sabi miɗo hoolii ko Laamɗo haalani kam koo, hono non jaati worrata,
44027026	kaa waajibi en njanoyan e ruunde.
44027027	E ley jemma sappo e nayaɓo oo, nde min ndoydata e geeci Adiriyatiki ndee, wakkati hejjere jemma donnooɓe laana kaa ɓee cikki ɓadike fanndude.
44027028	Ɓe tippii ɓoggol kaɓɓaangol ko teddi, ɓe tawi luggeendi ndii yo hakke darɗe noogay. Ɓe njehi yeeso seeɗa, ɓe tippii kasen, ɓe tawi luggeendi ndii yo hakke darɗe sappo e joy.
44027029	Ko ɓe kuli pati ɓe njanoy e kaaƴe koo, ɓe njippini torooje nay caggal laana kaa, eɓe ndoomi beetee.
44027030	Nde wonnoo donnooɓe laana kaa ɓee ana njiɗunoo soɓɓitaade, ɓe njippini laanawel pamarel ngel e ndiyam, ɓe mbii eɓe ɲiɓoya torooje to yeeso laana kaa too.
44027031	Pool wii mawɗo oo e sordaasi'en ɓee: --So yimɓe ɓee keddaaki e ley laana kaa, onon, on ndaɗataa.
44027032	Nden sordaasi'en ɓee taƴi ɓoggi nanngunooɗi laanawel pamarel ngel ɗii, njoppi ngel doyi.
44027033	Nde ɓadinoo weetude ndee, Pool ndaardi ɓe fuu ɓe ɲaama, wii: --Hannde woni balɗe sappo e nay oɗon kettii on ɲaamaali fay huunde.
44027034	Ɗum waɗi so miɗo ndaarda on ɲaamon, yalla oɗon ndaɗa, sabi fay gooto e mooɗon leeɓol hoore muuɗum solataa so saama.
44027035	Nde o haalnoo ɗum ndee, o ɓami buuru, o yetti Laamɗo yeeso maɓɓe ɓe fuu, o helti, o fuɗɗi ɲaamde.
44027036	Nden ɓe fuu ɓe ceyii, kamɓe duu ɓe ɓami ɓe ɲaami.
44027037	Minen wonɓe ley laana kaa ɓee, min yimɓe teemeɗe ɗiɗon e capanɗe njeɗɗon e njeegom.
44027038	Nde ɓe ɲaamnoo faa ɓe kaari ndee, ɓe ɓami caakuuji alkama gonɗi e laana kaa ɗii, ɓe tippii ɗi ley geeci yalla eɗum hoyfina ka.
44027039	Nde weetunoo ndee, ɓe coynii leydi, kaa ɓe annditaali ndi. Ɓe njii soɓɓundu e fonngo muuɗum. Ɓe kawri ɓe naɓan ton laana kaa so ɓe mbaawii.
44027040	Ɓe taƴi torooje ɗee, ɓe njoppi ɗe ley ndiyam ɗam, ɓe njorŋini ɓoggi kummbeeje gurfirɗe ɗee. Caggal ɗum, ɓe piilti wiir oo, ɓe ŋabbini ɗum to hoore laana too, yalla henndu nduu ana dunƴira ka yeeso. Ɓe peewi fonngo ngoo.
44027041	Ɓe porri e siwre, laana kaa higgi. Becce makka ɲiɓii e ley njaareendi ndii faa ka ronki dillinaade, bempeeje keli laaci makka.
44027042	Sordaasi'en ɓee anniyii warde kasunkooɓe ɓee pati fay gooto e maɓɓe yinoo so doga.
44027043	Kaa nde wonnoo mawɗo sordaasi'en oo ana yiɗi danndude Pool, haɗi ɓe waɗude anniya maɓɓe oo, yamiri waawɓe yinaade ɓee adoo fiyaade e ndiyam ƴeentoya,
44027044	heddiiɓe ɓee, yoga muuɗum'en nanngi bamuuje laana kaa, yoga nanngi taƴe makka. Hono nii ɓe fuu ɓe njottorii njoorndi e jam.
44028001	Nde min ndaɗi ndee, min nani ruunde ndee Malta wiyetee.
44028002	Hoɗuɓe ɗon ɓee njaɓɓorii min caahu mawɗo. Nde wonnoo oon wakkati kammu ana toɓa jaangol ana woodi, ɓe kuɓɓi yiite, ɓe njaɓɓii min faa min ƴuwloo.
44028003	Pool mooɓi leɗɗe, wedii e yiite ngee. Nguleefi kii yaltini e majje mboddi, ndi soppi junngo makko.
44028004	Nde hoɗuɓe ɗon ɓee njii mboddi ndii ana weelta e junngo Pool ndee, mbiyondiri e ko'e muuɗum'en: --Taƴoral oo gorko yo barɗo hoore, taweede o daɗii to geeci too fuu, hakkeeji makko ɗii accataa mo wuura.
44028005	O ficci mboddi ndii e yiite ngee, ɗum torraali mo fay huunde.
44028006	Ɓe miili o ɓuutan naa o saama ɗon e ɗon o maaya. Kaa nde ɓe kettinoo faa ɓooyi ndee, ɓe njii ɗum torriraali mo fay huunde, hakkillaaji maɓɓe mbaylitii e makko, ɓe mbii o gooto e laamɗo'en ɓee.
44028007	Publiyus, hooreejo ruunde ndee oo, ngesa muuɗum ana e sera nokkuure ndee. O jaɓɓiima min faa gasi, o jippini min, o saahii e amen, min ngaɗi to makko balɗe tati.
44028008	Hawri baaba Publiyus ana lelii sellaa, jontaaɗo, reedu muuɗum ana doga ƴiiƴam. Pool yehi to makko, duwii, fawi juuɗe muuɗum e makko, sellini mo.
44028009	Nde ɗum waɗunoo ndee, ɲawɓe wonɓe e ruunde ndee ɓee ngari, cellinaa.
44028010	Ɓe teddini min teddeengal manngal. Nde min njahata ndee, ɓe njooɓini min ko min kasindini e mum fuu.
44028011	Caggal lebbi tati, min naati e laana iwka Aleksandiri, ndabbunooka e ruunde ndee kaa, min mbitti. Eka ɲeɲaa ɲeɲugol Tooruuji Puneeji.
44028012	Min njottii ngeenndi mbiyeteendi Sirakusa, min ngaɗi ɗon balɗe tati.
44028013	Min naati ɗon, min takkii e fonngo geeci faa Regiyus. Janngo mum, henndu ɓaleeri wifi. E ley balɗe ɗiɗi min njottii Potiyoli.
44028014	Min tawi ton sakiraaɓe, ndaardi min paɓɓana ɗum'en yontere. Hono nii min njottorii Roma.
44028015	Nde wonnoo sakiraaɓe wonɓe Roma ɓee nanii garol amen, ngarii faa sakoro Abiya e nokku biyeteeɗo Jippule Tati sakkitaade min. Nde Pool yiinoo ɓe ndee, yetti Laamɗo, ɓeydorii cuusal.
44028016	Nde min njottii Roma ndee, Pool duŋanaa jippoo feere muuɗum, kaɲum e sordaasi kayboowo ɗum oo.
44028017	Balɗe tati caggal muuɗum, Pool noddi mawɓe Yahuudiyankooɓe. Nde ɓe mooɓtinoo ndee, o wii ɓe: --Sakiraaɓe! Mi waɗaali fay huunde ko luuttondirta kam e yimɓe meeɗen ɓee naa aadaaji njaatiraaɓe meeɗen ɗii, kaa mi nanngaama Urusaliima, mi wattaama e juuɗe Romankooɓe.
44028018	Nde ɓeen ƴeewi kabaaru am ndee, njiɗiino yoppude kam, sabi ɓe tawaali e am fay daliili gooto kaanɗo warde kam.
44028019	Kaa kammari Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee caliima mi yoppitee, ɗum waddani kam ɲaagaade sariya am ɓettinee naɓee to kaananke Roma mawɗo oo, tawee mi happaali leɲol am ngol fay huunde.
44028020	Ɗum waɗi so noddu-mi on yalla miɗo yiya on mi haalana on. Miɗo haɓɓorii ɗii calali saabe mo Israa'iilankooɓe pawi jikke e muuɗum oo.
44028021	Ɓe mbii mo: --Min keɓaali ɓataaki iwɗo Yahuudiya kaaloowo haala maa. Kasen duu fay gooto e sakiraaɓe ɓee waraali humpita min naa haala ko boni ko ngaɗ-ɗaa.
44028022	Kaa miɗen njiɗi kaalanaa min ko njii-ɗaa e hakkille maa, sabi miɗen anndi diina mo njokku-ɗaa oo ana luurraa ley nokkuuje ɗee fuu.
44028023	Ɓe cartanii mo nde ɓe ngartata. Ɲalaande ndee yottii, heewɓe ngari kawriti to jippunde makko too. Gila beetee kecco faa caggal kiraaɗe omo waajoo ɓe, omo fammina ɓe haala Laamu Laamɗo. Omo dallinoroo Tawreeta Muusaa e dewte annabaaɓe haala Iisaa.
44028024	Yoga e maɓɓe jaɓi ko o haali koo, yogaaɓe njaɓaali.
44028025	Nde ɓe caakotoo, tawi ɓe nganaa hawruɓe ndee, Pool ɓeydi hen konngol gootol, wii: --Ruuhu Ceniiɗo haalii goonga nde yottiniri haala annabi Esaaya, nde oon wii njaatiraaɓe mooɗon:
44028026	"Yaa to ngol leɲol mbiyaa ɗum: On kettinto faa palon noppi, kaa on paamataa. On ƴeewan faa puttinon gite, kaa on njiyataa.
44028027	Sabi ngol leɲol ɓernde mum yoorii. Ɓe cukkii noppi maɓɓe, ɓe mbumnii gite maɓɓe, pati gite maɓɓe njiya, pati noppi maɓɓe nana, pati hakkillaaji maɓɓe paama, sako ɓe ngarta mi sellina ɓe."
44028028	Pool jokkini hen, wii: --Anndee, kisindam Laamɗo neldaama ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe. Kamɓe ɓe kettinto! [
44028029	]
44028030	Pool waɗii duuɓi ɗiɗi kiɓɓi e ley suudu hasunoo nduu. Ɗon o silminannoo warannooɓe ƴeewde mo ɓee fuu,
44028031	omo waajoo Laamu Laamɗo, omo jannginira cuusal kabaaru Iisaa Almasiihu Joomiraaɗo oo, walaa kaɗuɗo mo.
45001001	Oo ɓataaki ga am iwri, miin Pool. Mi maccuɗo Iisaa Almasiihu, mi noddaaɗo faa mi laatoo nelaaɗo mum, mi cuɓaaɗo faa mi yottina Kabaaru Laamɗo Lobbo oo.
45001002	Oon Kabaaru Lobbo, Laamɗo fodiriino mo gila arannde annabaaɓe mum e ley Binndi ceniiɗi ɗii.
45001003	Kabaaru oo haala Ɓiyiiko haalata, iwɗo e Daawuuda banngal ɓii-aadamaaku mum,
45001004	banngal Ruuhu Ceniiɗo oo holliraa mo Ɓii Laamɗo Jom Baawɗe ko o immitii e maayde koo. Kanko woni Joomiraaɗo men Iisaa Almasiihu,
45001005	saabe makko keɓir-mi moƴƴere laataade nelaaɗo faa goonɗinɓe ɗowtaniiɓe mo keɓee ley leɲi ɗii fuu, yalla innde makko ndee ana teddinee.
45001006	Onon wonɓe Roma ɓee duu, oɗon njeyaa e maɓɓe, onon ɓe Laamɗo noddi faa kaɓɓo-ɗon e Iisaa Almasiihu ɓee.
45001007	Miɗo jowta on fuu, onon ɓe Laamɗo horsini, onon ɓe Laamɗo noddi faa laato-ɗon seniiɓe. Yo on keɓu moƴƴere e jam iwde e Baabiraaɗo men Laamɗo e Joomiraaɗo men Iisaa Almasiihu.
45001008	Ko adii fuu, miɗo yetta Laamɗo e innde Iisaa Almasiihu saabe mooɗon on fuu, sabi haala goonɗinal mon haalaama e aduna oo fuu.
45001009	Laamɗo mo ndewiran-mi ɓernde laaɓunde e ley ko njottinan-mi Kabaaru Lobbo haala Ɓiyiiko oo koo, o seede miɗo miccitoo on wakkati fuu
45001010	e ley duwaawuuji am fuu. Miɗo ɲaagoo Laamɗo newnana kam laawol e ley muuyɗe muuɗum no mi warda to mon.
45001011	Sabi miɗo yiɗi yiide on sanne, yalla ana daɲa ko njottin-mi on e dokkal ngal Ruuhu hokkata ngal faa ɲiiɓina on.
45001012	Mi ɓeyda hen: yalla goonɗinal ngal ndeentu-ɗen e mum ngal ana hokka en fuu semmbe.
45001013	Sakiraaɓe, miɗo yiɗi anndon: cili kuurɗi ngaɗu-mi anniya mi waran to mon, yalla ana daɲa ɓe keɓu-mi hakkunde mon no keɓir-mi yimɓe hakkunde leɲi goɗɗi ɗii nii, kaa faa jooni mi heɓaali warde.
45001014	Waajibi mi yaha to yimɓe fuu, jooɗiiɓe e ferɓe, jannguɓe e ɓe njanngaali.
45001015	Ɗum saabanii kam yiɗude yottinde on, onon Romankooɓe ɓee duu Kabaaru Lobbo haala Almasiihu oo.
45001016	Mi yaagortaako Kabaaru Lobbo oo, sabi o baawɗe Laamɗo, omo waawi hisinde goonɗinɗo mo fuu: Yahuudiyankooɓe tafon, caggal ɗum, leɲi goɗɗi ɗii duu.
45001017	Sabi Kabaaru Lobbo oo ɓannginta no Laamɗo nanngirta neɗɗo pooccitiiɗo yeeso mum --- goonɗinal tan waɗata ɗum, iwde e fuɗɗoode yaade e timmoode, no Binndi ɗii mbiiri nii: "Pooccitiiɗo wuurdan goonɗinal."
45001018	Tikkere Laamɗo ana ɓannga iwde dow kammu ana jippoo e yedduɓe e ooɲiiɓe fuu ɓe ooɲaare mum'en ɗeɗɗata goonga oo ɓee,
45001019	sabi ko neɗɗo waawi anndude e Laamɗo koo ana laaɓani ɓe, Laamɗo jaati ɓannginanii ɓe ɗum.
45001020	Sabi gila Laamɗo tagi aduna oo faa hannde, golle mum ana ɓanngina sifa mum mo yiyataake oo faa laaɓa, ɗum woni baawɗe makko faa abada ɗee e allankaaku makko oo. Saabe ɗum, yedduɓe mo ɓee ngalaa daɗirgal fey.
45001021	Fay so taweede eɓe anndi Laamɗo, ɓe teddiniraali ɗum no foti teddinireede nii, ɓe njettaali mo duu. Miilooji maɓɓe ɗii laatike ɓoli, fay ko ɓe anndi seeɗa koo duu niɓɓii.
45001022	Eɓe njaara ɓe hakkilante'en, kaa ɓe kaanɗii.
45001023	Ɓe loomtinirii teddeengal Laamɗo duumiiɗo oo tooruuji nannduɗi e yimɓe maayooɓe e pooli e daabaaji ɗi koyɗe nay e ɓoggi leydi.
45001024	Saabe ɗum, Laamɗo ɗaldi ɓe e coɓe no yonkiiji maɓɓe ɗii njiɗiri nii faa ɓe koyni terɗe maɓɓe, kamɓe e ko'e maɓɓe.
45001025	Ɓe loomtinirii Laamɗo goongaraajo oo fenaande, ɓe teddinii ko tagaa ɓe ndewii ɗum, ɓe njoppii Taguɗo oo. Yo jettooje ngoodan mo faa abada! Aamiina.
45001026	Saabe ɗum, Laamɗo ɗaldi ɓe e giɗaaɗe yonki maɓɓe kersiniiɗe. Rewɓe maɓɓe ɓee njoppii lelɗe worɓe mum'en ɗee, ndeentii e rewɓe hono mum'en faa woortondiri e no Laamɗo muuyrunoo ɗum nii.
45001027	Hono non worɓe ɓee duu njoppi waaldude e rewɓe faa ngatti muuyondirde. Worɓe ana ngaɗondira ko hersinii. Ɓe njukkaama kamɓe e ko'e maɓɓe jaati hakke majjere maɓɓe.
45001028	Saabe ko ɓe miijinoo anndude Laamɗo walaa ko nafata koo, Laamɗo ɗaldi ɓe e majjere maɓɓe, faa ɓe ngaɗi ko neɗɗo haanaa waɗude.
45001029	Ɓe ooɲiiɓe, ɓe ɓaleeɓe yonki, eɓe keewi joote e comndam fuu, kaɲum e haasidaaku e war-hoore e pooɗondiral e jammba e anniya bonɗo. Ɓe ɲo'ooɓe yimɓe,
45001030	ɓe ɲiŋooɓe yimɓe, ɓe waɲuɓe Laamɗo, ɓe hoynooɓe yimɓe, ɓe mawninkiniiɓe, ɓe mantotooɓe, ɓe seeɓanɓe ko boni, ɓe murtirɓe saaraaɓe maɓɓe,
45001031	ɓe ngalaa hakkille, ɓe nganaa hoolniiɓe, ɓe yoorɓe ɓerɗe, ɓe ngalaa yurmeende.
45001032	Fay so taweede eɓe anndi Laamɗo yamirii gaɗoowo hono ɗee kulle fuu ana haandi e maayde, ɓe kaaɗataa e waɗude ɗe tan, eɓe njaɓani duu gaɗoowo ɗe fuu.
45002001	Ndennoo, aan peloowo woɓɓe oo, ko mbaaw-ɗaa laataade fuu a walaa daɗirgal. Sabi so a felii woɓɓe tawi golle mooɗon yo gooto, a liɓii hoore maa.
45002002	Eɗen anndi Laamɗo ana sarira gollirooɓe hono ɗii golleeji ɓee ko waarata e goonga oo.
45002003	Hey! Aan peloowo gollooɓe hono ɗii golleeji ɓee tawee hono non ngollirtaa, tama aɗa sikki a daɗan sarri jukkungo Laamɗo ngoo?
45002004	Naa a jawɗo moƴƴuki Laamɗo mawki kii, kaɲum e muɲal mum e sawraare mum? Tama a anndaa Laamɗo ana holle moƴƴuki mum yalla aɗa tuuba?
45002005	Kaa ko a joorɗo ɓernde a caliiɗo tuubude koo, aɗa waddana hoore maa tikkere Laamɗo ɲannde Laamɗo ɓannginta tikkere mum e sariya mum pooccitiiɗo oo.
45002006	Sabi Laamɗo barjoto gooto fuu golle mum.
45002007	Tewtooɓe darja e teddeengal e ko duumotoo, tewtirooɓe ɗum muɲal ley golle lobbo ɓee keɓan nguurndam nduumiiɗam.
45002008	Kaa haasidi'en saliiɓe goonga so ana kaɓɓii e bonannda ɓee, jukkungo naawngo keɓata.
45002009	Torra e wemmbere ngoodanii gaɗoowo ko boni fuu: Yahuudiyankooɓe tafon, leɲi goɗɗi njokka hen.
45002010	Darja e teddeengal e jam ngoodanii gaɗoowo ko moƴƴi fuu, Yahuudiyankooɓe tafon, leɲi goɗɗi njokka hen.
45002011	Sabi Laamɗo ɓurdintaa yimɓe.
45002012	Laamɗo jukkan luuttooɓe ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe, fay so ɓe anndaa Sariya Muusaa oo. Kasen duu luuttooɓe so tawi ana anndi Sariya Muusaa oo, carirte Sariya oo.
45002013	Neɗɗo nanngirtaake pooccitiiɗo yeeso Laamɗo e hettinaade Sariya tan, jokkude Sariya oo waɗata so nanngiree pooccitiiɗo.
45002014	Ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee, kamɓe e waasude anndude Sariya Muusaa oo fuu, so ɓe ngaɗirii no Sariya Muusaa oo wiiri nii, ɓe kollii eɓe njogii sariya e ley hakkillaaji maɓɓe kamɓe e ko'e maɓɓe fay so ɓe ngalaa Sariya Muusaa oo.
45002015	Ɓe kollii ko Sariya Muusaa oo yamiri koo ana winndaa e ɓerɗe maɓɓe. Hakkillaaji maɓɓe ceediima ɗum, wakkatiiji eɓe anndi ley miilooji maɓɓe ɓe ngaɗii ko boni, wakkatiiji eɓe anndi ɓe ngaɗii ko moƴƴi.
45002016	Ɗum woni ko ɓanngoyta ɲannde Laamɗo yamirta Iisaa Almasiihu sara ko suuɗii ley ɓerɗe koo, sarira ɗum no Kabaaru Lobbo mo mbaajotoo-mi oo wiiri nii.
45002017	Aan, so a wii a Yahuudiyanke, a tuugike Sariya Muusaa oo, a mantorike Laamɗo,
45002018	aɗa anndi sago Laamɗo, a jannginaaɗo Sariya Muusaa oo faa mbaaw-ɗaa suɓaade ko moƴƴi,
45002019	a taƴorii a ɗowoowo wumɓe, a fooyre wonɓe e nimre ɓee,
45002020	aɗa waajoo ɓe njanngaali ɓee, aɗa janngina sukaaɓe saabe ko njogi-ɗaa anndal e goonga faa hiɓɓi e ley Sariya Muusaa oo koo ---
45002021	aɗa tinndina woɓɓe, ndennoo a tinndintaa hoore maa naa? Aɗa waajoo pati wujjee, a wujjataa naa?
45002022	Aɗa wiya pati jeenee, a jeenataa naa? Aɗa harmina tooruuji, a wujjataa ley to ɗi ndewetee too naa?
45002023	Aan mantortooɗo Sariya Muusaa oo, a luuttataa mo koynaa innde Laamɗo ndee naa?
45002024	Ɗum waɗi so Binndi ɗii mbii: "Onon ngaɗi so ɓe nganaa Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee ana mbonkoo innde Laamɗo ndee."
45002025	Sabi taadagol ana waawi nafude ma so aɗa haybi Sariya Muusaa oo, kaa so a yaaɓii Sariya Muusaa oo, a laatike hono mo taadaaki nii.
45002026	So mo taadaaki haybii jamirooje Sariya Muusaa ɗee, yalla waasude taadaade makko hiisataake no o taadiiɗo nii naa?
45002027	Mo taadaaki kaybuɗo Sariya Muusaa oo ana sare aan luuttuɗo Sariya oo, fay so a taadiiɗo annduɗo Binndi ɗii.
45002028	Sabi wanaa ko yiyetee koo waɗata neɗɗo Yahuudiyanke jaati, wanaa ko golletee e terɗe koo woni taadagol.
45002029	Ko yiyataake koo waɗata neɗɗo Yahuudiyanke jaati, taadagol duu ley ɓernde neɗɗo tawetee. E Ruuhu oo ɗum fawii, wanaa e binndi ɗii. Neɗɗo baaɗo non, wanaa yimɓe njettata ɗum, Laamɗo yettata ɗum.
45003001	Ndennoo, koɗum Yahuudiyanke ɓurdi leɲi goɗɗi ɗii? Koɗum woni nafaa taadagol?
45003002	Nafaa taadagol ana heewi e alhaaliiji ɗii fuu. Ko adii fuu, Yahuudiyankooɓe kalfinaa konngol Laamɗo ngol.
45003003	Kaa so yoga maɓɓe nganaa hoolniiɓe, ɗum ana waawi bonnude ko Laamɗo yo koolniiɗo koo naa?
45003004	Waawaa! Fay so yimɓe fuu yo fenooɓe, Laamɗo kaa yo goongirante. Sabi nii winndorii: "Fooccitaare maa ana annditee e ko kaalataa koo, so a sardaama a liɓan."
45003005	Ɗoo miɗo haalda no yimɓe nii: so ooɲaare men ana ɓeyda ɓannginde fooccitaare Laamɗo ndee, ɗum ana waɗa so mbiyen Laamɗo yo ooɲiiɗo so jippinii e men tikkere mum naa?
45003006	Fes! Sabi so Laamɗo yo ooɲiiɗo, hono o sarirta aduna oo?
45003007	So tawii fenaande am ana ɓeyda ɓannginde goonga Laamɗo oo eɗum teddina mo, saabe koɗum carirtee-mi mi luuttoowo?
45003008	Won ɲo'ooɓe en wiyooɓe eɗen mbiya: "Ngaɗen ko boni yalla ko moƴƴi ana funta hen." Ɓeen yimɓe, jukkungo mum'en ana foti e golleeji mum'en.
45003009	Ndennoo, enen Yahuudiyankooɓe ɓee, eɗen ɓuri heddiiɓe ɓee naa? En ɓuraa. Sabi mi hollii Yahuudiyanke e mo wanaa Yahuudiyanke fuu e ley luutti ngoni,
45003010	no Binndi ɗii mbiiri nii: "Walaa fuu pooccitiiɗo, fay gooto,
45003011	fay gooto walaa faamu, fay gooto tewtataa Laamɗo.
45003012	Yimɓe fuu yo majjuɓe, fuu yo bonɓe, walaa fuu gaɗoowo ko moƴƴi, fay gooto."
45003013	"Kunduɗe maɓɓe ana mba'i no janaale udditiiɗe nii, ɗemɗe maɓɓe ana mbowla pene bonɗe. Toni maɓɓe ana caawi tooke posoke."
45003014	"Haala maɓɓe fuu yo kuddi e konngi mettuɗi."
45003015	"Koyɗe maɓɓe ana njaawani yuppude ƴiiƴam,
45003016	bonannda e kunkoo ana jokki e maɓɓe to ɓe njahata fuu,
45003017	ɓe anndaa laawol jam."
45003018	"Kulol Laamɗo walaa e ɓerɗe maɓɓe fey."
45003019	Eɗen anndi huunde fuu ko Sariya Muusaa oo wii, wonɓe e ley mum ɓee haaldi, yalla kunduɗe fuu ana muɓɓoo, yimɓe aduna fuu paama potii e jukkungo Laamɗo.
45003020	Sabi fay gooto nanngirtaake pooccitiiɗo yeeso Laamɗo saabe haybude mum Sariya Muusaa oo, sabi walaa ko Sariya Muusaa oo waawi so wanaa anndinde yimɓe ko woni luuttal.
45003021	Kaa jooni Laamɗo ɓannginii no nanngirta yimɓe fooccitiiɓe ko wanaa haybude mum'en Sariya Muusaa --- no Sariya oo e dewte annabaaɓe ɗee ceedorii nii:
45003022	o nanngiran goonɗinɓe ɓee fuu fooccitiiɓe saabe goonɗinal mum'en Iisaa Almasiihu. Sabi walaa ko ɓurdini yimɓe:
45003023	yimɓe fuu luuttii, ngalaa ngeɗu e annoora Laamɗo.
45003024	Kaa Laamɗo nanngirii ɓe fooccitiiɓe meere meere kammari hinnee mum. O waɗii ɗum saabe Iisaa Almasiihu coottitiiɗo ɓe oo.
45003025	Oon Laamɗo fodi hokkitirde yonki mum faa yaafoo luutti goonɗinɓe ɗum, saabe ƴiiƴam mum ɗam. Hono non Laamɗo holliri fooccitaare mum, fay so jukkaalino luuttooɓe arannde
45003026	saabe muɲal mum. O waɗirii ɗum faa o ɓanngina fooccitaare makko wakkati mo ngon-ɗen e mum oo, yalla omo holla o pooccitiiɗo, kasen neɗɗo fuu goonɗinɗo Iisaa, o nanngiran ɗum pooccitiiɗo.
45003027	Ndennoo, koɗum fuu woni daliili wasu mo neɗɗo heddorii? Fay gooto! Haybude Sariya Muusaa oo saabii ɗum naa? Wanaa! Goonɗinal tan saabii ɗum!
45003028	Sabi miɗen anndi neɗɗo goonɗinal mum nanngirtee pooccitiiɗo, wanaa saabe haybugol mum Sariya Muusaa oo.
45003029	Naa Laamɗo yo Laamɗo Yahuudiyankooɓe tan? Wanaa kanko woni Laamɗo leɲi goɗɗi ɗii duu naa? Kanko jaati woni Laamɗo leɲi goɗɗi ɗii duu,
45003030	sabi Laamɗo gooto woodi, nanngiroowo taadiiɓe ɓee fooccitiiɓe saabe goonɗinal mum'en, ɓe taadaaki ɓee duu o nanngiran ɗum'en fooccitiiɓe saabe goonɗinal mum'en.
45003031	Ndennoo, min ittirooɓe Sariya Muusaa oo goonɗinal naa? Fes! Min ittaali mo, min tabintinɓe mo!
45004001	Koɗum mbiyaten e Ibarahiima njaati men oo?
45004002	So tawiino nii mo laatike pooccitiiɗo saabe golleeji makko ɗii, nden omo waawi mantaade. Kaa mo waawaa mantaade yeeso Laamɗo.
45004003	Sabi Binndi ɗii mbii: "Ibarahiima goonɗinii Laamɗo, Laamɗo jatorike mo saabe majjum mo pooccitiiɗo."
