66017016	Luwe sappo ɗe njii-ɗaa ɗee, kaɲum e taktakol ngol, mbaɲan bamfaaru rewru nduu, ɓola ɗum faa laaɓa heddoroo terɗe ɓole, ɲaama tew mum, nduppa ko heddii koo e yiite.
66017017	Sabi Laamɗo loowii e ɓerɗe maɓɓe waɗude anniya mum, ɓe laatoo daande wootere, ɓe ndokka taktakol ngol laamu maɓɓe, faa nde konngi Laamɗo ɗii fuu tabiti.
66017018	Bamfaaru rewru ndu njii-ɗaa nduu, kaɲum woni ngalluure mawnde huɓindiinde kaanankooɓe aduna.
66018001	Caggal ɗum, njii-mi malaa'ika goɗɗo keewɗo baawɗe ana iwa dow kammu ana jippoo, fooyre makko yaayni e aduna oo.
66018002	O eewnii faa toowi, o wii: "Nde halkiima! Baabila ngalluure mawnde ndee halkiima! Nde laatike hoɗorde seyɗaani'en bonɓe, suuɗorde ruuhu tuunnuɗo fuu e foondu tuunnundu waɲaandu fuu!
66018003	Sabi leyɗe ɗee fuu cigirii caamii saabe bamfaaraaku mayre oo, Kaanankooɓe aduna ɓee pijii e mayre, jaagotooɓe e aduna ɓee fuu keɓii jawdi saabe neemaaji mayre ƴaɓɓitiiɗi ɗii."
66018004	Non daande wonnde iwri kam dow kammu, ana wiya: --Njaltee e mayre, onon yimɓe am! Pati on ndeentu e mayre luutti, pati balaawuuji mayre hewta on.
66018005	Sabi luutti mayre njowondirii faa njottii kammu, Laamɗo rewtike golleeji mayre bonɗi ɗii.
66018006	Ngaɗiranee nde no nde waɗirani on nii. Njoɓto-ɗon ko nde waɗi on koo cowe ɗiɗi. Horde loonde nde nde siiwani on e mum ndee, ciiwanee nde hen cili ɗiɗi!
66018007	Jukkee nde, ngaɗee sugulla mayre hakke no nde teddiniri hoore mayre so nde wuuri e neema nii, sabi ende wiya e ɓernde mayre: "Mi kaananke debbo, mi wanaa debbo mo gorum maayi, abada mi wonataa e cuddu."
66018008	Saabe ɗum, e ɲalooma gooto balaawuuji mayre caamata e mayre: maayde e sugulla e yolbere, kasen duu nde duppete e yiite, sabi Joomiraaɗo Laamɗo caroowo nde oo yo Jom Semmbe.
66018009	Nde kaanankooɓe aduna reentuɓe e mayre jeenu so neemodii e mayre ɓee njii cuurki cumu mayre, ɓe mboyan, ɓe ɲonoto.
66018010	Ɓe toowtan nde ɓe ndaroo, saabe hulde jukkungo mayre pati hewtoo ɓe, eɓe mbiya: --Yoo yoy! Yoo yoy! Baabila, ndee ngalluure mawnde, ndee ngalluure jogiinde semmbe, e ley wakkati gooto tan, nde jukkaa!
66018011	Jaagotooɓe e aduna ɓee mboyan cuŋlanan nde, sabi fay gooto heddataako e soodude jaaguuji maɓɓe ɗii.
66018012	Jaaguuji maɓɓe yo kaŋŋe e cardi e kaaƴe dime e ɲaaƴe e bagiiji lobbi e bagiiji ciiɗi e bagiiji hariiri tiiɗuɗi e bagiiji boɗeeji e leɗɗe uurooje yogaaje e kaaki moƴƴiniraaɗi ɲiiƴe ɲiibi e kaaki moƴƴiniraaɗi leɗɗe tiiɗuɗe coggu e jamɗe kire e jamɗe ɓaleeje e haayre wiyeteende marba.
66018013	Jaaguuji maɓɓe kasen yo funngooji belnirɗi e uurnirɗi e gowe e nebam uuroojam e uurdi miira e uurdi suurtinteendi e peguujam e nebam ɓiɓɓe jaytuun e conndi alkama e na'i e baali e pucci e wotorooji e maccuɓe e ruggaaɓe.
66018014	Jaagotooɓe ɓee mbii ngalluure ndee: --Ko njiɗuno-ɗaa heɓude fuu woɗɗike ma: neema maa e dawla maa fuu halkike, a hewtataa ɗum abada kasen.
66018015	Jaagotooɓe heɓuɓe jawdi e mayre ɓee toowtan nde ndaroo to woɗɗi, saabe hulde jukkungo mayre ngoo pati hewto ɓe, ɓe mboyan, ɓe ɲonoto,
66018016	ɓe mbiyan: --Yoo yoy! Yoo yoy! Ngalluure mawnde parortoonde bagiiji lobbi e bagiiji ciiɗi e bagiiji boɗeeji, soɗortonoonde kaŋŋe e kaaƴe dime e ɲaaƴe!
66018017	E ley wakkati gooto tan, ɗee jawle fuu kalkaa! Dawranooɓe laanaaji ndiyam mawɗi ɗii ɓee e dawooɓe ɓee e summbooɓe ɓee, kaɲum e heɓooɓe nguure mum'en e lummbingol geeci ɓee, ɓe fuu ɓe toowtan ɓe ndaroo.
66018018	So ɓe njii cuurki cumu mayre, ɓe ngullan, ɓe mbiya: --Ngalluure honde nanndunoo e nden ngalluure mawnde?
66018019	Ɓe njooran leydi dow ko'e maɓɓe no ɓe poti metteede, ɓe mboyan ɓe ɲonoo, ɓe ngulla ɓe mbiya: --Yoo yoy! Yoo yoy! Ndee ngalluure mawnde, nde neema mum hokki jogiiɓe laanaaji e ley geeci fuu jawdi, e ley wakkati gooto tan, nde halkike!
66018020	Kammu, welta e halkeede mayre! Seniiɓe e nelaaɓe e annabaaɓe, onon duu mbeltee hen! Sabi Laamɗo sarii nde ko nde waɗi on koo!
66018021	E oon wakkati, malaa'ika jom semmbe ɓami kaaƴal nanndungal no niisirde mawnde nii, wedii ɗum semmbe ley geeci, wii: --Nii Baabila ngalluure mawnde ndee wedortee, nde yiyataake abada kasen!
66018022	Hankasen, fay gooto nanataa e mayre kolli hoɗooɓe gaaci e yimooɓe e puufooɓe cereeli e buutute, golloowo ɲeeɲuɗo fay gooto yiyataake kasen e ley mayre. Dillere unuɗe nanataake kasen e ley mayre,
66018023	fooyre lampa yaaynataa ley mayre kasen, jommbaajo gorko e jommbaajo debbo welɓe daaɗe maatataake e mayre kasen. Non worrata sabi jaagotooɓe mayre ɓurnoo aduna oo fuu doole. Kasen duu nde hoomtirii leɲi ɗii fuu mboŋobaaku mayre.
66018024	Ƴiiƴam annabaaɓe e seniiɓe e waranooɓe ley aduna oo ɓee fuu tawaama e mayre.
66019001	Caggal ɗum, nan-mi daaɗe toowɗe hono jamaa keewɗo iwri kam dow kammu, ana wiya: "Halleluya! Kisindam e teddungal e baawɗe ngoodanii Laamɗo meeɗen,
66019002	sabi sariyaaji makko yo goongaraaji yo pooccitiiɗi! O sarii bamfaaru rewru anndaandu sanne bonnirannoondu aduna oo fuu bamfaaraaku mum oo, kasen duu o yoɓtii ƴiiƴam maccuɓe makko njuppaaɗam e mayru ɗam."
66019003	Ɓe mbii ɗiɗoɓere: "Halleluya! Cuurki cumu ngalluure mawnde ndee kii ana ŋabba faa abada!"
66019004	Mawɓe noogayon e nayon ɓee e kuɗɗe nay guurɗe ɗee, kippii e leydi cujidani Laamɗo jooɗiiɗo e bimmbeere laamu oo, ana mbiya: --Aamiina! Halleluya!
66019005	Daande iwri to bimmbeere too, ana wiya: --Njettee Laamɗo meeɗen, onon maccuɓe makko fuu, onon hulɓe mo fuu, tedduɓe e lo'uɓe!
66019006	Non nan-mi ko wa'i no daande jamaa keewɗo nii, ko wa'i no dillere ndiyam keewɗam nii, ko wa'i no gidaali mawɗi nii, ana wiya: "Halleluya! Sabi Laamɗo Joomiraaɗo meeɗen Jom Baawɗe oo tabintinii laamu mum.
66019007	Mbelto-ɗen, ceyo-ɗen, teddinen mo, sabi kuurtungu Njawdiri ndii yottiima, kasen duu jommbaajo mayri lanndinike.
66019008	O hokkaama kaddule o ɓoornoo, bagi ɗaatuɗo, jalboowo, laaɓuɗo." Ɗeen kaddule ngoni golleeji seniiɓe moƴƴuɗi ɗii.
66019009	Malaa'ika oo wii kam: --Winndu: noddaaɓe e ɲiiri yannge Njawdiri ndii ɓee, mbelii hoore! O wii kam kasen: --Ɗii konngi yo goongaraaji, to Laamɗo ɗi iwi.
66019010	Kippii-mi e leydi yeeso makko faa mi sujidana mo, kaa o wii kam: --Patti! Miin, mi maccuɗo hono maa hono sakiraaɓe maa tiiɗuɓe e seettanaade Iisaa ɓee. Sujidan Laamɗo! Sabi ko woni annabaaku dee, yo seettanaade Iisaa.
66019011	Caggal ɗum, njii-mi kammu ana udditii, non puccu daneejo ɓanngi. Baɗɗiiɗo mo oo ana wiyee Koolniiɗo ana wiyee Goongirante, goonga o sarirta, goonga o honirta.
66019012	Gite makko ana mba'i no metangal yiite nii, tenngaaɗe laamu keewɗe ana e hoore makko, innde ana winndii e makko nde fay gooto anndaa so wanaa kanko.
66019013	Omo ɓoornii saaya cuuwaaka e ƴiiƴam, innde makko yo: "Konngol Laamɗo."
66019014	Konuuji kammu ɗii njokki e makko ana ɓoornii kaddule bagi ɗaatuɗe, daneeje, laaɓuɗe, ana mbaɗɗii pucci daneeji.
66019015	Kaafaawi mbelki ki mo soppirta leɲi ana yalta e hunduko makko. Mo durdan ɗi loocol naawngol, o dippan e ɓoosirde peguuje yaltinoore tikkere Laamɗo Jom Baawɗe mawnde.
66019016	Ndee ɗoo innde ana winndaa e saaya makko, ana winndaa e busal makko: "Kaananke kaanankooɓe e Joomiraaɗo joomiraaɓe".
66019017	Non njii-mi malaa'ika ana darii e dow yitere naange. O eewnii faa toowi, o wii pooli diwooji dow mbeeyu ɗii fuu: --Ngaree nootee ɲiiri yannge mawɗo mo Laamɗo waɗi oo,
66019018	faa nducciton tew kaanankooɓe e tew hooreeɓe sordaasi'en e tew jom'en semmbe e tew pucci e waɗɗiiɓe mum'en e tew yimɓe fuu --- rimɓe e riimayɓe, tedduɓe e lo'uɓe!
66019019	Non njii-mi taktakol manngol ngol e kaanankooɓe aduna ɓee e konuuji mum'en ana kawriti faa kaɓa e baɗɗiiɗo puccu daneejo oo e konu mum.
66019020	Taktakol ngol honaa, kanngol e annabaajo peneejo gannooɗo kaayɗe yeeso maggol oo. E ɗeen kaayɗe o hoomtirnoo heɓunooɓe maande taktakol ngol ɓee, sujidanannooɓe tooru nanndundu e maggol ɓee. Ɓe ɗiɗon fuu, ɓe mbedaa eɓe nguuri e weendu yiite e sitti huɓɓooru nduu.
66019021	Heddiiɓe ɓee kalkiraa kaafaawi njaltannooki e hunduko baɗɗiiɗo puccu daneejo oo kii, pooli ɗii fuu ngari nducciti tewuuli maɓɓe faa kaari.
66020001	Caggal ɗum, njii-mi malaa'ika ana iwa dow kammu ana jippoo, ana jogii e junngo mum cokitirgal ɓunndu yiite ndu luggeefi mum walaa ɗo haaɗi nduu, kaɲum e calalol manngol.
66020002	O nanngi kuungal ngal, ɗum woni mboddi aranndeeri mbiyeteendi Ibiliisa naa Seyɗaani ndii, o haɓɓi ɗum duuɓi ujunere.
66020003	O wedii ɗum e ley ɓunndu ndu luggeefi mum walaa ɗo haaɗi nduu, o uddi ndu dow mum, o meeli ndu, pati ngal ƴoɲɲa jaaleɲi faa nde duuɓi ujunere ɗii kiɓɓi. Caggal ɗum, ngal humtete wakkati seeɗa.
66020004	Non njii-mi bimmbeeje laamu. Jooɗiiɓe e majje ɓee ndokkaama baawɗe sarde. Njii-mi kasen yonkiiji ɓe ko'e mum'en taƴiranoo saabe ko ɓe ceettanii Iisaa koo e saabe ko ɓe mbaajii konngol Laamɗo koo. Ɓeen ngoni ɓe cujidanaali taktakol ngol e tooru nanndundu e mum nduu, ɓe keɓaali maande ndee e tiiɗe naa e juuɗe maɓɓe. Ɓeen nguurtii, laamodii e Almasiihu duuɓi ujunere.
66020005	Ɗum woni immital aranal ngal. Maayɓe heddiiɓe ɓee nguurtaali faa nde duuɓi ujunere ɗii kiɓɓi.
66020006	Malu e senaare ngoodanii jeyaaɓe e immital aranal ɓee! Maayde ɗiɗoɓere ndee walaa ko waawi e maɓɓe, ɓe laatanto Laamɗo e Almasiihu yottinooɓe sadaka, ɓe laamodoo e Almasiihu duuɓi ujunere.
66020007	So duuɓi ujunere ɗii kiɓɓii, Ibiliisa humtete yalta kasu mum,
66020008	faa ƴoɲɲa jaaleɲi gonɗi e paale aduna nay ɗee, ɗum woni garol Yaajuuju e Maajuuju, kaɲum e hawrintinde ɓe faa ɓe mba'a no njaareendi geeci kammari wolde.
66020009	Ɓeen yimɓe cankitii e aduna oo fuu, ɓe pilii ngalluure horsunde ndee, ɗo seniiɓe ɓee ngoni ɗoo. Oon wakkati fuu, yiite iwi dow kammu, halki ɓe.
66020010	Ibiliisa ƴoɲɲannooɗo ɓe oo wedaa e weendu yiite e sitti nduu, ɗo taktakol ngol e annabaajo peneejo oo ngoni ɗoo. Ɗon ɓe njukketee jemma e ɲalooma faa abada.
66020011	Caggal ɗum, njii-mi bimmbeere laamu mawnde raneere won jooɗiiɗo e dow mayre. Kammu e leydi fuu ndogi iwi yeeso jooɗiiɗo oo, ɗi njiitaaka kasen.
66020012	Njii-mi maayɓe ɓee, tedduɓe e lo'uɓe, ana ndarii yeeso bimmbeere laamu ndee. Dewte udditaa, e ley majje dewtere nguurndam ndee duu udditaa. Maayɓe ɓee cariraa golleeji mum'en binndaaɗi e dewte ɗee ɗii, gooto fuu hakke golle mum.
66020013	Geeci oo tottii maayɓe mum, maayde e laakaraa tottii maayɓe mum'en, gooto e maɓɓe fuu sariraa hakke golle mum.
66020014	Maayde e ko sabinbinta ɗum fuu mbedaa e weendu yiite nduu. Nduun weendu woni maayde ɗiɗoɓere ndee.
66020015	Neɗɗo fuu mo innde mum tawaaka ana winndii e dewtere nguurndam ndee, wedaama e weendu yiite nduu.
66021001	Caggal ɗum, njii-mi kammu keso e leydi keyri, sabi kammu arano oo e leydi aranndeeri ndii fuu iwii, geeci duu walaa.
66021002	Njii-mi Ngalluure Seniinde ndee --- ɗum woni Urusaliima keso oo --- ana iwa dow kammu to Laamɗo ana jippoo, ana parorii no jommbaajo parortoo faa lanndinoo hawra e gorum nii.
66021003	Nan-mi daande toownde iwrunde to bimmbeere laamu too, ana wiya: --Annii hoɗorde Laamɗo e yimɓe: o hoɗidan e maɓɓe, ɓe laatoo leɲol makko. Laamɗo e hoore mum wondan e maɓɓe, laatoo Laamɗo maɓɓe.
66021004	O soccan gonɗi gite maɓɓe fuu. Maayde e sugulla e gullaali e naawalla keddataako, sabi kulle ɓooyɗe ɗee fuu njawtii.
66021005	Jooɗiiɗo e bimmbeere ndee oo wii: --Mi heyɗintinan huunde fuu! O wii kam: --Winndu ɗii konngi fuu, ɗi celluɗi ɗi goongaraaji.
66021006	O wii kam kasen, --Huunde fuu biltike! Miin woni arano miin woni cakito, miin woni fuɗɗoode miin woni timmoode. Neɗɗo fuu ɗomɗuɗo, mi hokkan ɗum e sewnde ndiyam nguurndam ndee meere meere.
66021007	Neɗɗo fuu jaaliiɗo heɓan ɗum fuu, mi laatoto Laamɗo mum, laatoo ɓiyam.
66021008	Kaa rofeeɓe e ɓe ngalaa goonɗinal e soɓuɓe golleeji e warooɓe yimɓe e fijooɓe e boŋobii'en e rewooɓe tooruuji e fenooɓe ɓee fuu, weendu yiite e sitti huɓɓooru nduu woni ngeɗu mum'en. Ɗum woni maayde ɗiɗoɓere ndee.
66021009	Caggal ɗum, gooto e malaa'ika'en njeɗɗon jogiinooɓe le'e jeɗɗi keewɗe balaawuuji jeɗɗi cakitiiɗi ɗii wari, haaldi e am, wii: --War faa mi holle jommbaajo debbo, jom suudu Njawdiri ndii.
66021010	Non keew-mi Ruuhu, malaa'ika oo naɓi kam faa dow haayre mawnde toownde. O holli kam Urusaliima ngalluure seniinde ndee ana iwa dow kammu to Laamɗo ana jippoo,
66021011	annoora Laamɗo ana e mayre faa ende jalbira no haayre rimre nii, no haayre yaspe laaɓunde no timtorgal nii.
66021012	Tatawol tekkungol toowngol ana filtii nde, engol jogii dame sappo e ɗiɗi, damal fuu ana jogii malaa'ika. Cuuɗi baaba ɓiɓɓe Israa'iila sappo e ɗiɗi ɗii, inɗe mum'en ana mbinndaa e dame ɗee:
66021013	dame tati funnaange e dame tati hiirnaange e dame tati saahal e dame tati ɓaleeri.
66021014	Tatawol ngalluure ndee ngol ana fawii e dow kaaƴe sappo e ɗiɗi, wootere e majje fuu innde iwnde e sappo e ɗiɗon nelaaɓe Njawdiri ndii ɓee ana e mum.
66021015	Malaa'ika kaaldannooɗo e am oo ana jogii loocol kaŋŋe eenndirgol faa eennda ngalluure ndee e dame mayre e tatawol mayre ngol.
66021016	Tatteeji mayre nay ɗii fuu potu, njuunndi mayre e njaannji mayre potu. O eenndiri nde loocol ngol o joginoo ngol, nde laatii geɓe ujunaaji sappo e ɗiɗi (12,000), njuunndi ndii e njaannji ndii e tooweendi mayri fuu fotu.
66021017	O huulii tatawol ngol, ngol hawri e kuule teemedere e capanɗe nay e nay (144), huulagol ngol yimɓe kuulortoo ngol malaa'ika oo huulortoo.
66021018	Tatawol ngol yaspe mahiraa, ngalluure ndee kaŋŋe dimo baaɗo no timtorgal laaɓungal nii mahiraa.
66021019	Foomre tatawol ngalluure ndee ana pariraa sii kaaƴe dime fuu: aranndeere ndee yaspa, ɗiɗoɓere ndee safiir, tatoɓere ndee agate, nayoɓere ndee emerooda,
66021020	joyoɓere ndee sardoniksi, jeegoɓere ndee sarduwaan, jeɗɗoɓere ndee kirisolita, jettoɓere ndee berili, jeenaɓere ndee topaas, sappoɓere ndee kirisoparaas, sappo e go'oɓere ndee yasente, sappo e ɗiɗoɓere ndee ametiste.
66021021	Dame sappo e ɗiɗi ɗee yo ɲaaƴe luulu daneeje sappo e ɗiɗi, damal fuu ɲaayre luulu wootere moƴƴiniraa. Daalaare ngalluure ndee yo kaŋŋe dimo jalbiroowo no timtorgal nii.
66021022	Mi yiyaali suudu dewal e ley ngalluure ndee, sabi Joomiraaɗo Laamɗo Jom Baawɗe oo e Njawdiri ndii ngoni suudu dewal mayre.
66021023	Ngalluure ndee haajaaka naange naa lewru yaaynana ɗum, sabi darja Laamɗo yaaynata nde, Njawdiri ndii woni lampa mayre.
66021024	Jaaleɲi ɗii fuu e ley fooyre mayre njahata, kaanankooɓe aduna ɓee ngaddan e ley mayre jawle mum'en.
66021025	Jemma walaa e mayre, kasen duu dame mayre uddataako ɲalooma!
66021026	Ɓe ngaddan jawle e teddeengal jaaleɲi maɓɓe e ley mayre.
66021027	Huunde soɓunde naatataa e mayre, wanaa haala gollooɓe ko waɲaa, kaɲum e fenooɓe. Naatooɓe e mayre dee, ɓe inɗe mum'en mbinndaa e dewtere nguurndam ɓee, ɗum woni dewtere Njawdiri ndii.
66022001	Caggal ɗum, malaa'ika oo holli kam maayo ngo ndiyam mum hokkata nguurndam, njalbiroojam no timtorgal nii, eɗam iwra to bimmbeere laamu Laamɗo e Njawdiri ndii too.
66022002	Eɗam ila e hakkunde daalaare ngalluure ndee. Fonngooji maayo ngoo ɗiɗi fuu, lekki kokkoowi nguurndam ana e mum, ndimoowi cili sappo e ɗiɗi --- lewru fuu cilol. Haakolooji makki yo safaare sellinoore jaaleɲi.
66022003	Ko Laamɗo huɗi fuu, tawataake ley ngalluure ndee hankasen. Bimmbeere laamu Laamɗo e Njawdiri ndii darotoo e ley mayre, maccuɓe makko ndewan mo,
66022004	njiya yeeso makko, innde makko winndee e tiiɗe mum'en.
66022005	Jemma walaa hankasen, ɓe kaajataake fooyre lampa naa fooyre naange sabi Joomiraaɗo Laamɗo laatoto fooyre maɓɓe. Ɓe laamoto faa abada abadin.
66022006	Malaa'ika oo wii kam: --Ɗii konngi ana celli, ana ngoonɗi. Joomiraaɗo Laamɗo, loowuɗo konngol mum ley annabaaɓe oo, neli malaa'ika mum faa holla maccuɓe mum ko warata ɓooyataa.
66022007	Iisaa wii: --Kettinee, miɗo wara ɓooyataa! Neɗɗo fuu kaybuɗo ko woni e dewtere annabaaku ndee ɗoo, weli hoore.
66022008	Miin, Yuhanna, mi nanii mi yii kulle ɗee fuu. Caggal ko nan-mi e so njii-mi koo, kippii-mi e leydi yeeso malaa'ika kollannooɗo kam oo faa mi sujidana mo.
66022009	Kaa o wii kam: --Patti! Miin, mi maccuɗo hono maa hono sakiraaɓe maa annabaaɓe ɓee, kaɲum e haybooɓe konngi gonɗi e ndee ɗoo dewtere ɓee. Sujidan Laamɗo!
66022010	O wii kam kasen: --Pati suuɗu haalaaji annabaaku gonɗi e ndee ɗoo dewtere ɗii, sabi wakkati mo ɗum fuu ɗum laatotoo ɓadiima.
66022011	Gaɗoowo ko boni yo heddo e bonannda mum, coɓuɗo golleeji yo heddo e golleeji mum coɓuɗi ɗii, moƴƴo yo heddo e moƴƴuki mum, ceniiɗo yo heddo e senaare mum!
66022012	Iisaa wii: --Kettinee, miɗo wara ɓooyataa, miɗo waddora mbarjaari faa mi barjoo gooto fuu hakke golle mum.
66022013	Miin woni arano miin woni cakito, miin woni fuɗɗoode miin woni timmoode.
66022014	Loonnooɓe saayaaji mum'en yalla ana mbaawa ɲaamde e ɓiɓɓe lekki nguurndam kii e naatirde e ngalluure ndee damal, mbelii hoore!
66022015	Kaa wonɓe caggal mayre ɓee, ɓe dawaaɗi, ɓe boŋobii'en, ɓe fijooɓe, ɓe warooɓe yimɓe, ɓe rewooɓe tooruuji, ɓe fenooɓe e ley haalaaji e golleeji fuu.
66022016	Miin Iisaa, mi nelii malaa'ika am faa seettoo ɗee kulle e ley deente goonɗinɓe ɗee. Miin woni iwdi Daawuuda, mi taaniiko, miin woni hoodere fajiri jalboore ndee!
66022017	Ruuhu oo e jommbaajo debbo oo ndarii ana mbiya: --War gaa! Neɗɗo fuu nanɗo yo wii: "War gaa!" Neɗɗo fuu ɗomɗuɗo yo war, muuyɗo fuu yo yar e ndiyam ndokkoojam nguurndam ɗam meere meere.
66022018	Miin Yuhanna, miɗo jeertina neɗɗo fuu nanɗo konngi annabaaku gonɗi e ndee ɗoo dewtere ɗii: neɗɗo fuu ɓeyduɗo e majji huunde, Laamɗo ɓeydan e jukkungo joomum balaawuuji cifaaɗi e mayre ɗii.
66022019	Neɗɗo fuu taƴuɗo yoga e konngi ndee ɗoo dewtere annabaaku, Laamɗo taƴan goodi mum e lekki nguurndam cifaaki e mayre kii, kaɲum e ngalluure seniinde sifaande e mayre ndee.
66022020	Ceettantooɗo ɗeen kulle oo wii: --Taƴoral, miɗo wara ɓooyataa! Aamiina! War Joomiraaɗo men Iisaa!
66022021	Yo hinnee Joomiraaɗo men Iisaa wonu e mon on fuu!
